Current Commentary

Gandhi Imprisoned for the Third Time

Gandhi was arrested again in the Mumbai area on the fourth of this month. This is his third arrest. The first was in 1922, and the second was in 1930. In all three instances, he was arrested with extreme composure, submitting to capture without resistance. This attitude of peaceful submission, docility, and willingness to sacrifice is perhaps, as Tagore said, "His whole life is synonymous with sacrifice."

His arrest this time is because, after attending the Round Table Conference, he realized that the British government had no sincerity regarding Indian independence and prepared to revive the non-violent resistance movement. After returning to India, he even requested an audience with the Viceroy to discuss the matter. However, this peaceful request was met with a violent arrest.

Gandhi's arrest is not accidental. As capitalism enters its third stage and faces unprecedented turmoil and panic, it intensifies its exploitation of colonies to prolong its life. India is the outer treasury of the British Empire, the lifeblood of the British Isles. Currently, British capitalist imperialists are in a state of extreme panic and turmoil. The establishment of the Nationalist Government and the abandonment of the gold standard both prove that British imperialists are desperately trying to save their declining fate. At this time, to hope that they would lift India's shackles and allow Indian independence would only be done by the most foolish people in the world. The convening of the Round Table Conference and the discussion of the so-called constitutional issues are merely appeasement tactics. Gandhi's rashly going to London to attend was already a misstep, and his preparing to revive the non-violent resistance movement after returning to India made his arrest inevitable.

However, arresting one Gandhi cannot contain the surging tide of the Indian independence movement. On the contrary, the stimulus of Gandhi's arrest will further shatter the Indian people's illusion that the British imperialists will be merciful and allow their autonomy and independence. They will thoroughly recognize the true intentions of imperialism and become even more determined in their struggle. At the same time, it will make the Indian people realize that peaceful resistance is only a foolish policy and embark on another path of resistance and struggle. At this time, all opposing struggles are becoming increasingly acute. The independence movements of weak and small nations are expanding daily, and the high-pressure tactics of the suzerain states against independence movements are also becoming increasingly fierce. A great struggle is about to unfold. The battle between India and Britain is precisely the starting gun for launching this great struggle. Gandhi, when facing arrest, left a letter to the president of the All-India Congress Committee, Patel, saying, "Please tell the people of the nation never to abandon truth and the policy of non-violence." Before entering prison, Patel also issued a statement to the nation, saying, "May the whole country make noble sacrifices with a non-violent and full spirit." Non-violent resistance and peaceful struggle are Gandhi's consistent policies for resisting British imperialists. This policy has played a mitigating role in the Indian independence movement. George Bernard Shaw once said, "Britain conquered India with military force and suppresses India with military force. India can seize freedom with violence, just as Ireland gained freedom with military force." Shaw's words are correct. Whatever pure non-violence is effective, unless it is for foolish conservatism. Non-violent resistance and peaceful struggle to regain freedom from the hands of imperialists are like a docile sheep trying to use tears to get its beloved child back from the mouth of a tiger. Gandhi warned the Indian people not long ago, saying, "In the last struggle, Indians fought with sticks, but in this struggle, they may fight with guns." Gandhi is not unaware that the British government's suppression of the Indian independence movement will become increasingly severe and brutal. Yet he teaches the people of India to prepare for absolute non-resistance and to struggle against ruthless gunfire. Is this forgiveness to the enemy or cruelty to oneself? Romain Rolland once said, "He considers Gandhi a Christ who only lacks the cross." However, what does a non-resistant Christ have to offer to the liberation of the vast oppressed masses of India?

Nevertheless, Gandhi cannot be regarded as anything less than a great leader. His pure personality and philanthropic spirit have caused all the people of India to instinctively obey his orders and have caused people of all ethnic groups in India to instinctively respect him as "Mahatma." When he was imprisoned in Sabarmati Prison in 1930, an Indian newspaper had the following record: "In the evening, many people gather at Sabarmati Prison to pay their respects to their beloved leader. The masses stand in front of the prison as if standing in front of a temple. When they hear the bell ringing for people to visit prisoners, the masses are very happy. The people who come to admire him approach their revered Mahatma. Many kneel at his feet, many revere him, and many bow deeply in respect." Indeed, as Tagore said, "Gandhi is not only the greatest figure in India but also the greatest figure in the world today." Romain Rolland said, "This little man, as thin as a piece of wood, can mobilize 320 million people. He nods, he speaks a word, and it is an order. He is their God." Gandhi's greatness and nobility have already given us a true concept from the praises of his enemies and friends.

Although the liberation of India will ultimately not be realized under Gandhi's leadership, Gandhi still cannot be regarded as anything less than one of the greatest figures in the world.

Domestic Important Telegrams 2

Bandit Forces in Emou are Rampant

(Harbin) Emou County has been surrounded by bandits. Telegraph communication on the Jidun Road has been cut off since the 5th. Xi Qia has dispatched a regiment of troops to suppress them. (7th Special Dispatch)

National Salvation Movement Against Japan

(Nanjing) The Anti-Japanese Association of all circles in the capital, due to the total loss of territory in Northeast China and the imminent danger of Jehol, sent committee members Ni Guang and Luo Ciqi, among others, to the Central Party Headquarters on the 8th to petition for the swift dispatch of large armies to recover the lost territories. They also sent a telegram urging the three Central Committee members, Jiang, Hu, and Wang, to come to Nanjing immediately to jointly plan a national salvation and defense strategy. Central Committee member Ma Chaojun received them on behalf of the Central Committee and gave a satisfactory reply. They then went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to petition, where Gan Jiehou received them and also gave a considerable reply. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Fifty-three representatives from twenty-eight middle schools in Shanghai arrived in Nanjing on the 8th and are scheduled to petition the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 9th to promptly recover lost territories and protect sovereignty. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) More than 500 students from Jinling University went to the Executive Yuan to petition at 9:00 AM on the 8th. 1. Request the government to announce its diplomatic policy towards Japan immediately. 2. Explain the truth behind the Central Government's reply to Zhang Xueliang's telegram. 3. Is the secret loan agreement with Mitsui & Co. confirmed? 4. Request the government to provide substantial assistance to the Northeast generals. 5. Urge Wang, Jiang, and Hu to come to Nanjing immediately. Deputy Minister of Foreign Affairs Gan Jiehou replied to each item. Some students were still dissatisfied and decided to return to school and submit another request to the Executive Yuan for a written reply. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Jinling University students held a general meeting on the 8th and resolved: 1. Send a telegram to the whole country, stating that any secret traitorous treaty that has not been recognized by the people will not be recognized. 2. Telegraph Wang, Jiang, and Hu to come to Nanjing immediately to face the national crisis together. 3. Warn Hu Hanmin to abandon old grievances, forget personal interests for the sake of the country, and promote unification. (8th Special Dispatch)

The Case of the Assault on the American Consul in Harbin

Japan Apologizes and Settles the Matter

(Washington) Secretary of State Stimson announced today that the U.S. government has accepted Japan's apology for the assault on Chamberlain, an official of the American Consulate, by Japanese soldiers. The case is now closed. Initially, American public opinion believed that the U.S. government was completely dissatisfied with Japan's report on the matter, but according to today's statement by the authorities, all misunderstandings have been eliminated. (7th Reuters Dispatch)

Central Discussions

The Case of Establishing New Agencies in Guangdong

(Nanjing) The Central Party Headquarters held a discussion meeting this morning and afternoon. It is said that there was a discussion on the establishment of the Southwest Executive Department in Guangdong. (7th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) A certain Central Committee member said that Wang Jingwei's resignation was due to illness and his inability to come to Nanjing, fearing that some would accuse him of being unwilling to take responsibility. However, the Central Committee will definitely try to persuade Wang to stay. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) A certain important figure in Guangdong stated that the Southwest Executive Department's Political Committee, Military Committee, and three agencies are based on proposals by Hu, Sun, and Wu, and were implemented without consulting Hu beforehand. If other provinces do not have similar organizations and party and national leaders do not approve, these three agencies can be abolished and will definitely not be used to disrupt peace. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Sun Jiafang, a member of the Guangdong faction, went to Nanjing to discuss the allocation of surplus customs revenue to subsidize Guangdong's military and administrative expenses. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Executive Department members Chen Jitang, Deng Zhiru, and Xiao Focheng sent a telegram on the 7th urging Li Zongren to return to Guangdong to open the Southwest National Defense Conference. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Xiao Focheng said on the 8th that Wu is determined to take the position of Chairman of Guangdong, and Hu has not gone to Nanjing, nor has he scheduled a return to Guangdong. The Southwest Conference will be held in Guangdong after Li Zongren and others arrive. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Li Yangjing resigned as a Standing Committee member of the Executive Department. The two newly established agencies in the Southwest had not yet officially opened for business on the 8th, and Xiao also claimed to be ill. (8th Special Dispatch)

The Beiping Political Affairs Committee Holds a Meeting

(Beiping) The Beiping Political Affairs Committee held a meeting this afternoon at Prince Shuncheng's Mansion. Zhang Xueliang and all committee members in Beijing attended and discussed public security in North China. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) More than 3,000 students who fled from the Northeast to Beiping are living in extreme poverty and are requesting assistance from the authorities. Zhang Xueliang raised this issue for discussion at today's meeting of the Political Affairs Committee, and all agreed to find ways to provide assistance. (Entry Day Special Dispatch)

Chen Gongbo Will Go to Beiping

(Beiping) Chen Gongbo is scheduled to come to Beiping the day after tomorrow, bearing a mission from the central government, to have contact with Zhang. (8th Special Dispatch)

Zhang Xueliang

Decision to Reduce Military Spending

(Beiping) A certain foreign newspaper reported this morning that there have been rumors recently that Zhang Xueliang is about to resign. According to reliable sources, this is not true. However, as the situation in the Northeast becomes increasingly tense, he has repeatedly expressed the necessity of actively uniting with generals from all sides to maintain public security in North China. After the establishment of the new government, Zhang still maintains his usual attitude. Due to financial difficulties, he hopes that the new government can formulate a financial plan under the centralized tax revenue to maintain local needs. The military expenditure in the North is insufficient by one million. Zhang has decided to cut administrative expenses by 20%, starting with the Northeast Army. This plan will be announced soon. The Beiping Military and Financial Affairs Committee has decided not to establish a chairman and will have committee members from the two committees take turns serving as chairman. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Military Affairs Committee has been established, with Zhang Xueliang as chairman, responsible for handling all military affairs in the North. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) People here expect that Zhang Xueliang may withhold customs and salt taxes from Tianjin. Local Chinese officials regard the rumors that Zhang Xueliang will resign soon as absolutely untrue. It is said that Zhang has announced his intention to continue to support the central government but hinted that the financial agreement between Beiping and Nanjing may undergo some changes. Due to financial difficulties, Zhang has no choice but to divert certain taxes belonging to the central government for his own use. It is generally believed that he intends to intercept customs and salt taxes from Tianjin. (8th Reuters Dispatch)

Establishment of a Political Branch in Taiyuan

(Beiping) It has been resolved to establish a political branch in Taiyuan, with Yan Xishan as chairman, based on the principle of stabilizing the North. Zhang has telegraphed the central government for instructions. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Taiyuan) The official received a telegram from Beijing stating that the central government will establish a Northwest Political Branch in Taiyuan, appointing Yan as chairman. An official order may be issued within days. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Taiyuan) Yan is ill in his hometown, and visitors have not been received. (8th Special Dispatch)

Education in Beiping Comes to a Standstill

(Beiping) Education in Beiping is bankrupt. From universities to primary schools, everything is at a standstill. Various schools owe 1.85 million yuan, equivalent to five months' worth. Representatives from seven schools, including the Normal University Women's College, went to Beijing today to demand back pay from the Ministry of Finance and Education. If there is no effective solution, all faculty and staff are prepared to go to Beijing to sit-in and demand payment. All primary and secondary schools in the city have continued to suspend classes. Representatives from various secondary school faculty and staff went to the Municipal Government today to demand salaries. If there is no satisfactory reply, it has been decided that all faculty and staff will go to the Municipal Government to sit-in and demand payment. (8th Special Dispatch)

Gan Generals

Requesting Sun Weiruyi to Preside Over Gansu

(Beiping) A telegram from Lanzhou states that Shao Lizi has firmly declined the position of chairman of Gansu. All the generals are supporting Sun Weiruyi to preside over Gansu. Headed by Chen Guizhang, a telegram has been sent to the central government requesting immediate appointment. The Gansu Provisional Political Affairs Committee has resolved on thirteen important cases for military and administrative reorganization. Sun Weiruyi plans to carry them to Yang Hucheng in Shaanxi in person, requesting approval for implementation separately. (8th Special Dispatch)

Liu Guo and Other Units March on Foot

Heading Towards Dakouwen

(Jinan) Liu Guitang, Guo Mafeng, and other units have marched on foot from Dabian Bridge towards Dakouwen, but they request: 1. Do not send armored vehicles and troops to monitor them. 2. After the incorporation at Dakouwen, march on foot to Gaotang by cart. 3. Treat them leniently at the beginning of the incorporation. Han has telegraphed Liu's representative, Xia Ziming, to come to Jinan for discussion. (8th Special Dispatch)

Bandit Forces in Huangpi Subside Slightly

(Hankou) Huangpi bandits have been suppressed by the combined efforts of Xia Douyin, Xu Tingyao, and Xiao Zhichu, as well as by aerial bombardment. It is reported that they have subsided slightly on the 8th. Han's brigade and Peng's brigade of Xu Yuanquan's unit, and Li Mingzhong's division, are all in the counties of Huangma. Han's brigade departed from Hekou Xinji and captured Luo Jiatian. Peng's brigade captured Dasheng Mountain. There have been no changes in Baliliwan in southern Huang'an. It is rumored that the bandits still intend to launch a general offensive within a week. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) Xiao Zhichu remained in Wuhan due to illness. He has telegraphed Deputy Division Commander Hua Wenxuan to pay special attention to the defense of the southern section of the Pinghan Railway. Hua replied that he has dispatched troops to Wangjiadian, Santu Bu, and Zhujiawan to block and defend. The safety of Pinghan transportation is ensured. Furthermore, the Pacification Headquarters ordered four air squadrons to send two aircraft north daily to bomb the bandits. According to reports, the bandit forces are not likely to expand. (7th Special Dispatch)

The National Government Routine Meeting Was Canceled Yesterday

(Nanjing) The National Government's routine meeting on the 8th was canceled because many committee members were scattered in various places and had not yet taken office. (8th Special Dispatch)

The Preparatory Sound of the National Crisis Conference

(Nanjing) The Preparatory Committee for the National Crisis Conference met at the Central Party Headquarters on the afternoon of the 8th to discuss preparatory matters. (8th Special Dispatch)

Staff of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission Demand Back Pay

(Nanjing) Staff of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission sent a letter to former Chairman Ma Fuxiang, urging the payment of back pay for November and December of last year and the refund of construction fees for the Central Party Headquarters. (8th Special Dispatch)

Domestic Important Telegrams 3

The Issue of the Number of Legislative Yuan Members

However, there are currently 63 members of the Legislative Yuan. It remains to be studied how to reduce the number of members by 13 to meet the determined quota. (8th Special Dispatch)

Plan to Improve Domestic Debt Bonds

(Nanjing) Domestic public bond holders recently requested to convene a national economic conference to seek an overall improvement plan. Minister of Finance Huang Hanliang has been in contact with financial and economic experts and the banking community in Shanghai to determine whether such a gathering is necessary. Now that a unified government has been established, it is imperative to foster civil rights and protect public opinion to meet expectations and demonstrate impartiality. All censorship of telegrams and news should be abolished immediately, and the Executive Yuan is directed to instruct all competent authorities to earnestly comply. This is of utmost importance. This order also appointed Wu Shangying as Political Vice Minister of the Ministry of Finance and Lin Kanghou as Permanent Vice Minister of the Ministry of Finance. Foreign News

Korean Patriot Attempts to Assassinate Japanese Emperor Unsuccessful

Hand Grenade Mistakenly Hits Accompanying Vehicle

Lee Bong-chang Arrested on the Spot

Inukai Cabinet's Resignation Not Approved

Reuters, Tokyo, 8th - This morning, when the Japanese Emperor was returning to the palace after the New Year's inspection, near the Sakuradamon gate in front of the palace, a Korean suddenly threw a bomb that hit the accompanying vehicle. The explosion was very loud and shocked everyone. Fortunately, no one was injured, only a horse was slightly injured. The assailant was arrested on the spot. He was identified as a Korean named Asayama, 32 years old. After being taken to the police station, he was searched and another bomb was found in his pocket. The motive for the attack has not been revealed, but it is believed to be inspired by the resurgence of the Indian independence movement. The police authorities believe that the Korean may have been impulsive because of the recent reports of the Indian non-violent resistance movement. The Cabinet offered its resignation this afternoon because the Emperor's entourage was attacked, but the Emperor ordered Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi to continue to serve as usual, pending further instructions. It is believed that the Emperor will consult with his advisors and may accept the Cabinet's resignation. It is reported that after interrogation, the assailant admitted that the two bombs were supplied by the Provisional Korean Government in Shanghai, and he was also given 300 Japanese yen.

National, Tokyo, 8th - The Japanese Cabinet has tendered its resignation, led by Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi, due to the assassination attempt on the Japanese Emperor by a Korean. Inukai entered the palace and presented the Cabinet's resignation to the Emperor at around 5:00 PM today, expressing that the Seiyukai party bears full responsibility for this incident. This kind of resignation is actually just a formality, because it is not enough to express the Japanese people's respect for the imperial family. As for the Korean who assassinated the Japanese Emperor, he is a nationalist, from Seoul, named Lee Bong-chang (transliteration). At 11:45 AM this morning, when the Emperor was returning to the palace after reviewing the troops, he threw a hand grenade at the Emperor's car, but failed to hit the Emperor's car, and it only exploded next to the third accompanying vehicle. The car was slightly damaged, but there were no injuries. The Emperor returned to the palace safely, and the Korean was arrested on the spot. He is currently under strict surveillance and may soon face the death penalty. Since the Japanese army invaded the eastern provinces of China, the Indian national revolutionary movement has followed, and the restoration movement within Korea has shown a vigorous trend. The police authorities were ordered in advance to take strict precautions, so after this incident occurred, the authorities immediately conducted a thorough investigation to see if there were any accomplices.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 8th - When the Japanese Emperor was returning to the palace after the military review this afternoon, near Sakuradamon, at the corner in front of the Kojimachi Ward Sakuradacho Police Station, a Korean named Lee Bong-chang, renamed Kinoshita Shozo, 32 years old, living in Tokyo's Nishikicho, threw a hand grenade at the Emperor when the Emperor's car was about to enter the gate. Fortunately, the car was moving fast and the bomb fell on the second carriage of the attendants, none of whom were injured. The Emperor was extremely frightened and almost fell out of the car. The perpetrator was arrested on the spot.

Form Asian Alliance

Jointly Defend Against Aggression by Great Powers

Britain, France, and Italy Pay Close Attention

Paris News - According to reports from Angola in various newspapers, the five countries of Soviet Russia, Turkey, Persia, Afghanistan, and Iraq have recently formed an Asian alliance and decided to send representatives to Angola in mid-January of this year to hold a formal meeting to complete the plan. Its purpose is to jointly defend against imperialist aggression. The countries of the Near East are the gateways to Soviet Russia. As for the weak nations such as Turkey, Persia, Afghanistan, and Iraq, they have long been subjected to the infringement of the Western European powers. Their interests are related, so they have to cooperate with each other. The realization of this plan is a major success for Soviet Russia's Near East diplomacy. Britain, France, Italy, and other countries are paying close attention to the organization of the alliance. Regarding the organization of this alliance, Soviet Russia originally adopted a secret policy, but it was only recently discovered by various countries. (World News Agency)

All India Congress

New President Arrested Again

Authorities Block Economy to Curb Chaos

Avoid Reckless Use of Force Against Mobs

Reuters, Bombay, 8th - Dr. Ansari, Acting President of the All India Congress, was arrested here today, further restricting the activities of the Congress. It is reported that members of the Congress plan to attack government salt warehouses, which will be the most serious development. If implemented, the government will take severe measures to deal with it. The Illegal Societies Act was implemented in the Dexing Province today. Red posters were posted on the walls of the Bombay Empire Building, with fierce slogans threatening British officials, which are said to have been made by the Hindustan Republican Association.

Reuters, Bombay, 8th - The police are still engaged in the search and arrest of the leaders of the All India Congress, but today they also discussed adopting a new method of dealing with them, planning to notify those concerned, prohibiting them from speaking at Congress venues, and requiring them to report their daily activities to the police station. Violators will be sentenced to two years in prison. It is reported that the legal advisor of the All India Congress is now considering presenting a petition to the High Court to send Gandhi to the court for trial, so as to debate whether the imprisonment is justified. The government is now planning to find ways to block the economic sources of the All India Congress, causing it to be in trouble due to lack of funds. Judging from the situation, the government is now willing to try its best to avoid using force against the mobs and to use economic martial law to curb the activities of the Congress. The government is taking a policy of arresting the leaders of the All India Congress on the one hand, and trying to avoid using police batons against the masses on the other hand, and only using them when necessary, so as to avoid sending many injured people to the hospital. This policy already has signs today. There are crowds watching the picket team and the road is blocked. In normal times, the police would disperse them with batons, but now they only gently persuade them to give way to the side of the road. The Governor-General announced the invitation to several important leaders of the moderates to hold a meeting. Some people in several circles believe that the Governor-General intends to convene a conference of political leaders of India. In fact, this is not the case. India only wants to meet with several representatives who participated in the Round Table Conference. During the meeting, of course, it is necessary to discuss the overall situation caused by non-violent resistance. However, the main purpose is to solicit figures in the constitutional field in order to facilitate the work of the investigation committee that will arrive in India soon. There is now an application for the Governor-General to convene a conference of parts of the community willing to cooperate with the government as soon as possible to discuss the best way to implement the constitutional progress program set by British Prime Minister MacDonald.

Public Telegram

The Hubei Flood Relief Committee Begs for Donations Telegram to the Shanghai Shenbao Newspaper: The severity of the floods in Hubei this year is unprecedented in a century. This committee started emergency relief work in early summer, thinking that it could be concluded by autumn and winter. Unexpectedly, the number of disaster victims in Wuhan is increasing, and the hardship is even more serious than during the emergency relief period. In summer, they can sleep outdoors, but now the weather is cold and freezing, and they must have rooms or sheds. In summer, they can go out and in barefoot, but now it is raining and snowing, and the north wind is howling. The wealthy are not warm even in heavy furs, and those who survived the disaster are mostly unable to cover their bodies with clothes. Therefore, every time the sky is overcast, the stiff are lying on the road, and people are ordered to bury them everywhere. Coffins are nowhere to be bought. The official dams and civilian embankments of the counties have been breached and collapsed, and they are all in sight. If you want to repair them, there is no way to start. The most bitter thing is that the houses that were flooded in Daoguang Wushen and Jiyou have not been restored for eighty years. This year's flood has flooded villages, and most of the houses have been destroyed and turned into ruins. If they enter the mountains, they have long been occupied by Red bandits, and if they return home, they have lost their base early. There is no way to advance or retreat, and the only way is to rush to Wuhan. As of the end of the national calendar year, those who have been given relief by this committee in turn have registers to check. In the Wuchang area, Hongshan, Luojia Mountain, Meizi Mountain, Changchun Temple, and areas outside the Dadongmen still have more than 200,000 disaster victims. In Hanyang, there are 108,000 disaster victims in Hushan alone. Hankou is double that of Wuyang, so in terms of the three towns of Wuhan, the monthly expenditure is not less than 400,000 yuan. Now we have tried our best to deal with it for six or seven months. Chang'an is not easy, and the coming day will be difficult. The colleagues of this committee have been running around and calling for help, their voices are hoarse and their lips are worn out, and there is no way to save them. We want to do it, but we can't. As for the previous emergency relief, when we first started, we hired ships, built sheds, distributed rice, provided medical care, and salvaged floating corpses. We responded in a hurry and started on a grand scale. The funds were all scraped together from the east and west. Now that the end of the year is coming, it is not easy to clear the accounts and ask for loans. The daily food consumption of each shelter, and the relief of each disaster-stricken county, Wuhan needs to pay 10,000 to 20,000 yuan per day. Each county receives rice, clothes, and wheat, ranging from tens of thousands to thousands. As for the request to repair dams, there are 50 counties listed, and it will cost tens of millions to repair the leaks. A group of elders said that the great floods in Daoguang Wushen and Jiyou, if the embankments that have collapsed this year are not repaired, will repeat the mistakes of the Daoguang era. Thinking of the future, we cannot help but shudder. We only hope that the benevolent and righteous people in various provinces and ports will spread the word, develop compassion, pity these survivors, and lead them to the shore, encourage them to donate, beg for help, and collect cheap springs and collect righteous grains. The saying goes, doing good deeds has blessings, and doing good deeds brings auspiciousness. At this time of renewal of the old year, we hope to spread the warmth of spring and gather a sum of money to save a part of the people. Donate one yuan more, and save one more life. Accumulate good deeds and have remaining blessings, and may good intentions prolong life. The disaster victims are grateful to the world, and the colleagues are also eager to help. If the fundraising is successful, it will still be remitted to the Wuhan General Chamber of Commerce and received by this committee. The receipt will be sent at any time and compiled and published for public information. Hubei Flood Relief Committee, He Chengjun and others.

Therefore, it is necessary to establish a Central Executive Department, Political Affairs Committee, and Military Commission in Guangdong today to engage in the suppression of the Communist bandits, consolidation of national defense, and promotion of autonomy. The significance of today's establishment is even greater and more celebratory. Brothers often feel that Chinese people have a habit that every New Year, they must say good words and auspicious words, such as "Happy New Year" and "Everything Goes Well", and such as New Year couplets, they often write "San Yuan Kaitai Everything is Renewed" and "Good Weather, National Peace and People's Security" and other words, although they belong to the empty talk of the old people, but in the final analysis, there is also something to be taken, such as "Everything Goes Well", that is, every citizen has the happiness of freedom and equality, "Everything is Renewed", that is, the Republic of China has achieved the goal of a lifetime, and the country is peaceful and the people are safe. Today is the New Year's Day, and I have a word to say to all comrades, that is, in this most serious situation, we must have the fighting spirit of the Prime Minister, unite sincerely, and take on the Prime Minister's responsibility of saving the country and the people. Then, we will not fail the Prime Minister's trust, and we will not fail the people's expectations. That is the meaning of today's memorial. After the report, the group worship ceremony was held, and each other bowed. After the group worship was completed, the swearing-in ceremony of the three institutions was held immediately. The person swearing read the oath with his right hand raised, and all the committee members present served as witnesses. After the swearing, slogans were shouted, photos were taken, and a tea party was held to disperse. In the afternoon, they went to Yantang to hold a large review to show celebration.

The three institutions started working on the 4th. The list of candidates for committee members who have been announced is as follows: 1. Hu Hanmin, Chen Jitang, Bai Chongxi, Liu Jiwen, Chen Ce, and Li Yangjing are the six standing committee members of the Southwest Executive Department of the Central Executive Committee. Liu Jiwen is the Secretary-General, Chen Jitang is the Director of the Organization Group, Lin Zhimian is the Director of the Propaganda Group, and Xiao Focheng is the Director of the Overseas Party Department. 2. Li Zongren, Chen Jitang, Bai Chongxi, Zhang Fakui, Li Pinxian, Ye Qi, Liu Xing, Zhang Huichang, Chen Ce, Yu Hanmou, Xiang Hanping, Li Yangjing, Li Fulin, Xue Yue, Xu Jingtang, Miao Peinan, Zhu Huiri, Lu Tang Shaoyi, Deng Zheru, Xiao Focheng, Liu Jiwen, Wu Chaoshu, Lin Zhimian and other twenty-seven people are members of the Southwest Military Commission of the National Government. Chen Jitang is the chairman of the committee, and there are no standing committee members. 3. Tang Shaoyi, Deng Zheru, Xiao Focheng, Chen Jitang, Li Zongren, Wu Chaoshu, Chen Ce, Liu Jiwen, Lin Yun Huang Xuchu, Zhang Huichang, Chen Rong, Li Xiaosheng, Ma Junwu, Zou Lu, Lin Zhimian, Lin Jizhong, Feng Zhuwan, Yang Xixu, Li Pan, Cheng Tianhui, Luo Yiqun, Ou Fangpu, Wu Shangying and other twenty-seven people are standing committee members of the Political Affairs Committee. Anti-Japanese Demonstration Held by Hunan Students

Fourth Route Army Generals Telegraph Request to Punish Japan

Changsha Correspondence: Since the fall of Jinzhou, the bad news has spread, and the 30 million people of Hunan are extremely indignant. They have telegraphed leaders such as Chiang, Wang, and Hu one after another, requesting them to go to Beijing as soon as possible to jointly face the national crisis. The Hunan Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association also gathered students from various schools at the Provincial Education Association Square this morning (the 6th) to hold a solemn and enthusiastic street demonstration rally. More than 50 schools participated, with about 20,000 people. After the ceremony, Chairman Huang Dingqing first reported the purpose of the meeting, and then proposed various petition items for discussion. As a result, the entire body passed the following resolutions: 1. Request He Jian to implement the proposal to the Fourth Plenary Session, to recover lost territory by force, and to jointly telegraph the National Government with military and political leaders across the country, ordering a general mobilization; 2. Oppose all local organizations; 3. Jointly telegraph the whole country, requesting Wang, Chiang, and Hu to go to Beijing in the near future to preside over the party, government, and military affairs; 4. The whole country should unite to resist Japan; 5. Support the national salvation government; 6. Request the issuance of firearms to students of various schools, and a nationwide general mobilization to depart for the Northeast; 7. Request He Jian to rectify provincial administration. After the decision, Tan Changkai of the Provincial Party Committee, Yao Xuehuai of the Municipal Party Committee, and others successively delivered speeches, hoping that everyone would unite, work hard, and jointly face the national crisis to save the country from danger. After the speeches, they lined up and set off to Dongchang Street and Limen Street, to the Fourth Route Army Headquarters, where they submitted the petition. He Jian personally came out to reply, expressing acceptance. After leaving the General Headquarters, they passed through Ganziyuan, Qingshi Bridge, Denglong Street, Huangdao Street, Nanzheng Street, to the Provincial Government to petition. Secretary-General Yi Zhuzhu received them and promised to forward the petition for implementation. Then they left the Provincial Government, passed through Sijinwan, Zhuanpozi Street, Hongpailou, Bajiaoting, Zoumalou, Nanyang Street, Fuzheng Street, Lao Zhaobi, Youyicun, and returned to the Education Association Square to disband the meeting, which was already 2:00 PM.

The generals of He Jian's Fourth Route Army were also extremely indignant at the Japanese atrocities. They telegraphed the Central Government, requesting an early decision and the determination of a major plan, and declared that their troops were fully armed and awaiting orders. The original telegram is as follows: "To Chairman Lin of the Nanjing National Government, Premier Sun of the Executive Yuan, Minister He of the Military and Political Affairs Department, and Chief of Staff Zhu Junjian: The violent Japanese have invaded and occupied the eastern provinces for several months. All those with blood and qi are furious. Jian previously made suggestions to the Fourth Plenary Session and party and government leaders, believing that the Sino-Japanese issue must be resolved by force to save the country and survive. Even world peace and international justice cannot rely solely on empty words; we must first defend and strengthen ourselves in order to gain sympathy and shift the argument. It is unexpected that while the people of the country are working hard to unite, the violent Japanese continue to invade. The isolated army in the eastern provinces has been fighting for a long time, with exhausted ammunition and no reinforcements. The bad news has come that Jinzhou has been attacked and captured, and they are driving straight in, shocking Pingjin. The tragic disaster of national subjugation is imminent. I believe that even a trapped beast fights, and with our 400 million descendants of the Yellow Emperor, how can we not rise up and strive to annihilate those island barbarians? Only hesitation and procrastination are the enemies of action. Now that the country is peaceful and unified, there is no room for delay in resisting foreign aggression. The gentlemen of the Central Government, having shouldered the heavy responsibility of saving the country and wiping out humiliation, must have good plans for internal stability and external defense. We should request an early decision and the determination of a major plan, on the one hand, strictly ordering the front line to recover lost territory, and on the other hand, broadly raising funds and equipment to meet the situation. Jian respectfully leads his troops, waiting for dispatch, with a keen sense of patriotism, daring not to choose words. Fully armed and awaiting orders, Fourth Route Army Commander He Jian, 28th Army Commander Liu Jianxu, 15th Division Commander Wang Dongyuan, 16th Division Commander Peng Weiren, 19th Division Commander Li Jue, 59th Division Commander Zhang Ying, 62nd Division Commander Tao Guang, 63rd Division Commander Chen Guangzhong, Newly Compiled 34th Division Commander Chen Quzhen, Xiangqian Border Defense Commander Wang Jialie respectfully kowtow (January 6th)."

Joint Suppression of Bandits in Huangpi by Land and Air Forces

The Bandits Claim 40,000, but in Reality, There Are Only Over 10,000

Troops from the Xu and Xia Divisions Are Blocking at the Front Line

The Pinghan Railway Is Still Peaceful and Vehicles Pass as Usual

Hankou Correspondence: The Xiaodian, Hekou, and Changxuanling areas in the northern part of Huangpi County have long been bandit dens. Because they have not launched a large-scale invasion to the south, people have generally taken it lightly. After Li Mingzhong was appointed as the Pacification Commissioner of the Henan-Anhui-Hubei Border Area, the county was划into the defense zone, and the Commissioner's Office was also set up there. The people, with a large army stationed there, were even more fearless. Unexpectedly, after the fall of Huang'an on the 22nd of last month, Kuang Jixun joined forces with the bandits in the northern part of Huangpi County with three divisions and one brigade, invading southward in successive waves, and their momentum was almost unstoppable. The county seat of Huangpi was also in imminent danger. The place is only more than 60 miles away from Hankou. If Huangpi is not defended, the bandits can reach the border of Hankou directly in half a day. The citizens are in fear and anxiety, informing each other in panic. After the reporter investigated various parties, it was learned that the bandits were still five miles away from the county seat of Huangpi. Although the bandits claimed to have 40,000 troops, there were only over 10,000 in reality. There were not enough rifles, only several thousand, and ammunition was very scarce. There was also an airplane, named Liewu, but because there were no bombs, it was only used for reconnaissance. The leader, a certain Ouyang, was also quite fierce. Kuang himself was still unknown where he was. The government troops who advanced to suppress the bandits included two regiments of Xiao Zhichu's 44th Division, two regiments of Xia Douyin's 13th Division, one brigade and two regiments of Xu Tingyao's 4th Division, and two regiments of Ge Yunlong's 33rd Division. The Xia troops set off from Qijiawan, and the Xu troops set off from Hankou, and both had rushed to the front line, engaging in fierce battles with the bandits for several days. The Ge troops were stationed in the county seat, and the Xiao troops were stationed to defend the railway, encircling the bandits in an arc. The Hubei Pacification Commissioner's Office also ordered the 4th Aviation Team to dispatch two combat aircraft, Douglass and Morse, carrying heavy bombs, to assist in the suppression. On the 6th and 7th, the two aircraft dropped many bombs in the vicinity of Huangpi and the bandit nests in Huang'an, killing many bandits. According to reports, the bandit's momentum would not expand. As for the situation of the fierce battle in the front, no detailed reports have been received here. However, according to the military telegrams and the reports from people in Huangpi, the government troops have indeed succeeded, and the bandit's momentum is gradually weakening. The county seat of Huangpi is very solid, because the Xu and Xia divisions are both elite troops, and even if the bandits are brave, they will not be able to cross the Leichi Lake one step. As for the traffic on the southern section of the Pinghan Railway, it is maintained by the Xiao Zhichu troops. Xiao himself stayed in Hankou due to illness. Fearing that the bandit's momentum would disrupt the railway, he telegraphed Hua Wenxuan, the deputy commander of the division, to pay special attention. On the 7th, he received a reply telegram from Hua, saying that troops had been dispatched to Wangjiadian, Zhujiawan, Sanchabu, and other places for defense, and the traffic was extremely safe. Combining the news from various sources, Huangpi is not in any danger, and the people here are gradually settling down. However, the disaster victims from various places who have been fleeing to Hankou in recent days are shoulder to shoulder. Three days ago, there were only more than 100,000 people, but on the 7th, it had increased to 300,000. The Garrison Command, fearing that bandits might be mixed in, has strictly ordered its subordinates to conduct thorough investigations, especially paying attention to the disaster victims in Huangpi, so as to prevent bandits from destroying the security of Wuhan. (January 7th)

Bandit Forces in Fujian, Jiangxi, and Guangdong Borders Still Fierce

Many Refugees Flee to Guangdong Province

Shantou Correspondence: After the Red Bandits of southern Jiangxi, Peng, Dian, Zhu, Li, and other groups, captured Huichang, the people on the Fujian-Jiangxi border followed the militia and moved into the Fujian-Guangdong border. Ouyang Xin, the chairman of the Huichang Local Maintenance Association, went to Xitouxu in Wuping, recruited troops, and obtained three large teams, which were merged into the Ministry of Zhong Wencai in western Fujian to continue resisting the bandits. The militia of Huichang, Ruijin, Anyuan, Xunwu, and Yudu counties retreated to the Pingyuan County area on the Guangdong border due to the strength of the Red Bandits, while the refugees supported the old and carried the young, fleeing to Guangdong. The Jiangxi militia jointly elected Xie Jiayou as the commander-in-chief and Ouyang Jiang as the deputy commander-in-chief, and set up a temporary bandit suppression headquarters office in Niudouguang on the Xunping border. Xie had old grudges with Zhong Wencai of Wuping, and it was a pity that they could not cooperate in suppressing the bandits at this time. Also, Ouyang Xin arrived in Shantou yesterday to ask the Second Division Headquarters for assistance in funding and ammunition. Xie Jiayou also sent personnel to Shantou to ask for assistance after taking office as the bandit suppression officer in Niudouguang. Commander Zhang, believing that the Jiangxi bandits were rampant and intended to break into the Fujian-Guangdong border, allocated a large amount of ammunition and distributed it to Zhang Ying's camp in Pingyuan and the Jiangxi militia for replenishment. At present, the entire territory of Pingyuan is still very peaceful, but Jiaoling County is showing signs of unrest. Many villagers moved to the county seat, and the teachers and students of the school were scattered. In addition, Yongding County in Fujian Province, since it was captured by the Red Bandit Zhang Dingcheng, almost the entire county has become a Red area. The bandit then spied on Dabu and advanced to Fengshi, using seven civilian boats to cross the river. Fortunately, they were repelled by the militia. The troops stationed in Dabu, He Yuguang and Liang Ruogu, prepared to send teams into Fujian to suppress the bandits because the Red Bandits often invaded. Also, the 2,000 Red Bandits of Peng Dehuai's Ministry in southern Jiangxi harassed Guikengxu and Dayang Bridge in Wuping. Zhong Qiangui's Newly Compiled Independent First Brigade of the Guangdong Army advanced to block and suppress them. They fought fiercely with the bandits in Guikeng for three hours. The bandits were almost wiped out, and four water machine guns and more than a hundred rifles were captured. Sixty-six Red Bandits were captured alive, and more than a hundred bandits were killed. The bandits fled to Junmenling, so the county was not disturbed by the Red Bandits, which was also fortunate among misfortunes.

Educational News and Headlines

Zhou Fo-hai, Director of Education of Jiangsu Province, Proposes

Solutions to Educational Funding Problems

"Provincial Committee Yesterday Passed the Suspension of Payment of Assistance Fees to Central University

Educational Funding Committee Scheduled to Hold Meeting

Zhou Fo-hai, the new Director of Education of Jiangsu Province, has been in office for several days. The reporter paid a special visit yesterday, and the following is a record of his conversation: (Question) When will the Director hold the inaugural ceremony? (Answer) It needs to be reported to the Provincial Government. (Question) It has been reported recently that Jiangsu schools have an organization to demand salaries. What policies are there for the future educational funding problems in Jiangsu? (Answer) The purpose and scope of the salary demand plan is only for the salaries of teachers and staff, which is not a fundamental problem. I am now planning to propose to the Provincial Government to seek a fundamental solution to educational funding. If it is only for salaries, even if it is resolved temporarily, it is not a permanent solution. (Then he showed the reporter the proposal). (Question) It is said that the Educational Funding Management Committee will hold a meeting soon. Is there a fixed date? (Answer) It will be held around the 12th. Wu Zhilao and Niu Tilao have both sent letters promising to attend at that time.

Zhou Fo-hai Proposes to the Provincial Government

Zhenjiang, 8th Electric News: Zhou Fo-hai proposed to the Provincial Government to suspend the payment of Central University's assistance funds from January of the 21st to allocate all of them to the educational funds of Jiangsu Province. It was passed at the Provincial Committee meeting on the 8th.

Zhou Fo-hai's proposal to the Provincial Government is as follows: The educational funding of this province is extremely tight and has reached its limit. It is proposed to forward it to the two ministries of Finance and Education, and refer to the method of allocating funds to Wuhan University from the national tax revenue within Hubei Province. All the funds of Central University should be allocated from the cigarette tax revenue within Jiangsu Province in full. In the future, all the income of the Jiangsu Educational Funding Management Office should be allocated to the educational undertakings of the province. Is it appropriate? Please make a public decision. Committee member and Director of Education Zhou Fo-hai proposed: It is found that the funding for the National Central University was previously stipulated by the Central Government to be allocated from the educational funding of Jiangsu Province at 1.32 million yuan per year to offset the expenditure. Over the years, the Jiangsu Educational Funding Management Office has tried its best to bear the burden, but due to the vastness of the provincial educational undertakings and the shortage of funding sources, the income and expenditure of provincial educational funding are not in balance, and there is a deficit every year. The educational funding of Jiangsu Province has always relied on the special cigarette tax as a major and reliable source of income. Previously, the Central Government resolved to transfer the special tax revenue to the Central Government and designated 1.8 million yuan to be allocated from the land tax revenue of Jiangsu to offset the deficit. When the income is insufficient, the Ministry of Finance will still allocate the full amount from the cigarette tax. However, because the land tax income varies from year to year, and the collecting agencies often embezzle educational funds and arbitrarily reduce the amount when responding to the Ministry of Finance's requests for funds, the amount of the special land tax funds underpaid from the 16th to the 19th year reached more than 2 million yuan. Repeatedly requested the Ministry of Finance to fulfill the previous agreement and allocate the full amount from the cigarette tax revenue, but it has not been implemented. As a result, the income and expenditure of the Jiangsu Educational Funding Office in the past three or four years have increased year by year. This year, the famine has spread throughout the province, and the income has been further reduced. It is estimated that the total annual income and expenditure, together with

Zhou Fohai, Director of Education for Jiangsu Province

The previous deficit of nearly three million yuan, coupled with the recent accumulation of debts for various agency expenses, has left the management office utterly impoverished. If relief is not swiftly sought, the funding for National Central University will undoubtedly become unsustainable, and the educational endeavors of the province will also grind to a halt. Previously, we received the Central Government's promulgated budget regulations for the 19th year of the Republic trial implementation and the budget management standards issued last November, which clearly delineate the boundaries between national and local revenue and expenditure. The sources of Jiangsu Province's educational funding, namely the land tax and the slaughter tax, are classified as local revenue according to the classification standards. Meanwhile, the funding for national universities should be classified as national expenditure. Using local revenue to support national expenditure was acceptable when local finances were relatively abundant and had surplus capacity. However, the educational finances of this province have reached a point of exhaustion. If we are forced to bear this enormous expenditure, bankruptcy is imminent. At that time, National Central University and the provincial educational institutions will inevitably meet their demise. Fohai, having been appointed to oversee the entire province's education, from the very beginning of his tenure, recognizing the urgent need to stabilize funding for Jiangsu's education in order to establish a foundation for its endeavors, and also acknowledging that National Central University, as the nation's highest institution of learning, should be strongly supported, proposes to request that the Ministries of Finance and Education be consulted to follow the precedent of Wuhan University, where funding is allocated from Hubei's national tax revenue. All funding for National Central University should be designated from Jiangsu's cigarette tax revenue and allocated in full. Subsequently, all revenue of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Funding Management Office will be used to fully fund provincial educational affairs. This way, the funding for National Central University can be secured, and the deficit in provincial school funding can be more easily addressed. Your decision on the appropriateness of this proposal is respectfully requested.

No Need to Correct Confucius' Birthday

The Ministry of Education replied to the Executive Yuan, stating that the Ministry of Education will continue to designate the 27th day of the eighth month of the solar calendar as Confucius' Birthday Memorial Day, and there is no need to correct it. The letter responded to the Executive Yuan's secretariat, stating: "Regarding the Hunan Provincial Government's submission from the Director of the Guiding County Education Bureau, requesting a correction of Confucius' Birthday to emphasize commemoration and facilitate sacrifices, which was forwarded by the Ministry for investigation, along with a copy of the original submission. The original Confucius' Birthday Memorial Day was set as the 27th day of the eighth month of the lunar calendar. In December of the 17th year of the Republic, the Ministry, considering that the National Government was promoting the solar calendar and the lunar calendar was inconvenient to use, requested the Academia Sinica to calculate the corresponding date in the Gregorian calendar for the 17th day of the eighth month of the lunar calendar in the 21st year of the reign of King Zhao of Zhou. The Executive Yuan's eighth meeting resolved that Confucius' Birthday Memorial should be set as the 27th day of the eighth month of the solar calendar, and the Ministry followed this resolution and promulgated it. For several years, there has been no perceived inconvenience. Furthermore, converting lunar dates to solar dates is not unique to Confucius' Birthday Memorial; the Martyrs' Day commemorating the Seventy-Two Martyrs and the Lantern Festival and Dragon Boat Festival, which are based on the lunar calendar, are also replaced with the same month and day in the solar calendar. Although this does not match the original dates, the people have not found it awkward. In addition, the Ministry's revised regulations for the school year, semesters, and holidays stipulate that elementary schools' summer vacation starts on July 3rd and ends on August 21st, middle schools' summer vacation starts on June 30th and ends on August 24th, and colleges and universities' summer vacation starts on June 23rd and ends on August 31st. Therefore, on August 27th of the solar calendar, elementary and middle schools have already started, and although colleges and universities have not yet started, the start of the semester is near, and most teachers and staff have returned to school. The original submission's claim that schools are mostly empty during the summer vacation does not align with the facts. Based on the above reasons, the Ministry believes that there is no need to correct Confucius' Birthday Memorial Day. Your review and further instructions are respectfully requested."

China Education and Culture Foundation Board of Directors

Sixth Regular Meeting Held Yesterday

Six Important Proposals Passed

Jiang Menglin and Zhao Yuanren Resign

The China Education and Culture Foundation Board of Directors, established with funds returned by the United States from the Boxer Indemnity, held its sixth regular meeting yesterday morning at 9:00 AM at the Licha Hotel. The directors present included Vice Chairman Jiang Menglin, Chinese directors Wu Chaochu, Hu Shi, Ren Hongjun, Zhao Yuanren, and American directors Gu Lin, director of the Union Hospital, Situ Leideng, president of Yenching University, Baker, advisor to the Ministry of Communications, and Bernard, general manager of Citibank, totaling nine individuals. Chairman Cai Yuanpei was absent due to illness and was represented by Vice Chairman Jiang Menglin. During the morning session, reports were given by the honorary secretary, honorary accountant, the auditing committee of the executive committee, and the executive director of the foundation. The afternoon session began at 2:00 PM and passed six important proposals: (1) Accepting the construction of one of the major buildings for the National Peiping Library Construction Committee; (2) Establishing a financial advisory committee, appointing Shanghai financial experts Xu Xinliu, Gu Yiqun, and Bernard as committee members, with the task of guiding the foundation's investment endeavors; (3) Passing measures to end the foundation's established science professorships and the science professors' sabbatical program; (4) Regarding the special funding for joint research between the foundation and National Peiping University, which was approved last year, the funding is at risk of being suspended this year due to Peiping University's financial difficulties. The board of directors passed a resolution today that, regardless of whether Peiping University can pay on time, the foundation should still allocate the twenty thousand yuan of joint funding for this year on schedule; (5) Regarding the construction costs of the National Central Research Institute's physics, chemistry, and engineering research institute, the foundation previously donated five hundred thousand yuan. This year, due to soaring gold prices, an additional one hundred and twenty thousand yuan is needed to complete the project. A resolution was passed to continue subsidizing sixty thousand yuan to help complete the project; (6) Jiang Menglin resigned from his position as a director to avoid suspicion, and Zhao Yuanren resigned to take up the position of supervisor of Tsinghua's American students in the United States. Both resignations were approved, and Xu Xinliu and Zhou Yichun were elected to succeed them as directors. It is reported that the directors left Shanghai after the meeting.
