Free Talk

Talks by the Idle Man - Removing the Courtyard Grass

Talking About Education From Burning a Coal Stove (Part 1)

When I was young, I ate ready-made meals cooked by my mother every day. Sometimes I would go to the kitchen to take a look, like a popular graduation tour. I never lifted a finger, so I wasted more than thirty years and simply didn't know what a stove was all about. I saw that my mother could burn it very easily, so I thought it was really easy and that I could do it with just a glance. Why bother to do it myself?

Starting with the belief that I could do it with a glance and ending with a lifetime of not knowing how, I realized this strange thing when I was thirty-five years old. That year, a poor friend was preparing to cook for me for lunch. I volunteered to light the stove for him, but I was badly defeated. He washed and chopped the vegetables, but I hadn't even lit the fire. I had no choice but to give way to the capable and let him take care of everything. He lit the fire in a moment. I asked him the secret, and he said, "To light the stove, you need to use burning charcoal as kindling." Hearing this, I suddenly realized that it contained an important principle. From then on, using advanced students to guide new students became an important method for me over the years.

In 1927, I started to burn a fire a few times. At that time, we used thatch. Thatch is easy to light and easy to extinguish. As soon as it lights, it bursts into a ball of fire and turns into ashes. I put bundles of thatch into the stove, and I couldn't leave for a moment. If I left, the fire would go out. You have to keep sending thatch in to maintain the flame. Burning thatch is such a waste of energy!

Miscellaneous Records of Peculiar Surnames

— Cicada Shedding

The Shen Bao's local news on the 30th contains a list of names of the All-China Islamic representatives going to India to pay homage to the Kaaba, including Mai Cheng-zhang, Shi Yu, and Cheng San. Aren't these two surnames, Mai and Shi, very peculiar? When I was at the Pukou Weighing and Inspection Bureau, there was a Mai Qiu-fan, who was from Jiayu County, Hubei Province. According to Qiu-fan, "There are only two branches of the Mai surname in all of China: one in Nanjing and one in Jiayu. As for how the Mai surname originated, it was around the Sui and Tang dynasties, when people from U-Tsang moved to Ningxia in China." According to the U-Tsang route, business was very prosperous during the Sui and Tang dynasties. The Tang Dynasty monk Xuanzang went to India to study Buddhism and reached India via U-Tsang. The Mai surname in Nanjing is quite wealthy and has always started from business since generations ago. "Notes from the Small Sky Juniper Hall" states, "There was a Huai Army commander named Zhe Gui. When he first joined the army, people asked for his surname, and he said, 'I have no surname.' He was a beggar on the streets who lost his parents when he was young, so he didn't know his surname. Later, he accumulated merit and was promoted to a recorded Brigadier General. When the memorial was being drafted, Hefei asked him, but he also said that he didn't know his surname. Hefei said, 'How can a general have no surname?' The commander asked Hefei to give him a surname. Hefei was reading official documents and said, 'You can recognize a word,' pointing to the word 'Zhe' in 'Respectfully Report.' Therefore, he took this as his surname." According to the notes, the surname Zhe came about through recognition, and there is no such surname in the "Book of Ten Thousand Surnames." However, I remember that when my uncle Shengjie, the censor, was inspecting the southern city, he was ordered to investigate those in charge. All officials and servants had to drink a cup of wine and smoke a tube of tobacco before they could perform their duties. At that time, there was a yamen runner named Zhe Biao, who saw that everyone else had a fearful expression. Zhe Biao stepped forward and drank three large cups of wine because Zhe Biao was a famous drunkard. For these few days, he had no money to buy wine, and his enthusiasm was ignited. He drank the official wine to his heart's content. Also, there was a runner named Zhe Biao in Wu County, Suzhou. When Sai Jinhua was exiled to Wu County, the local officials were ordered to keep her under strict surveillance. Zhe Biao was the runner in charge of surveillance. However, Sai Jinhua was replaced by someone else at the time of her exile. At that time, Zhe of Wu County was Li Zi'ao. Li was from Sichuan and had a marital relationship with my family. One day, he was drunk and incited Zi'ao to summon Sai Jinhua to the case for inspection. My initial intention was just a playful gesture. Who would have thought that the Sai Jinhua who arrived was a substitute? Zi'ao was furious and severely punished Zhe Biao, ordering him to hand over the original person. At that time, Sai Jinhua was already in Shanghai. Hearing that this move was at my instigation, she came to my residence to ask me what I thought. I got to know Sai Jinhua's true face and met this leader of Jianghu heroes. I then wrote a letter to Zi'ao to exonerate him. Later, I moved my home to the Dragon Prestige Cave in Taihu, only to realize that Zhe Biao's power was not to be insulted. Now that I see the Zhe surname in the Shen Bao as a large Islamic surname, it is possible that the Zhe Gui in "Notes from the Small Juniper Hall" is a mistake in the transmission. Also, "Good Friend Magazine" has Lao Yanruo, a Chinese manufacturer, with the "Lao" surname which is also very peculiar, so I am appending it here.

World Anecdotes

— Haike

Two Great Thieves: There is a French master car thief named Camille Debauche. According to his own account, he stole as many as 307 cars in three years. His calm demeanor is truly astonishing. Once, he stole a car on a main street in Paris and drove away at full speed. Unexpectedly, someone saw him and gave chase. Later, at an intersection, he was blocked by countless vehicles and could no longer escape. Helpless, he stopped the engine, draped his coat over one arm, and stood by the car. He immediately told the police officer that the car thief had run away, and since he saw no one in the car, he was guarding it on behalf of the owner until it could be handed over to the police station. The police officer even raised his hand in salute to him, never knowing that he was the car thief himself. America also has a great thief named George Dlkinson. He came from a wealthy family and did not worry about food or clothing. During the day, he worked as a clerk in a shirt factory, but in the evenings, for excitement, he would go out and commit theft. Every week, he would go out four or five times to lead his life as a burglar. He was eventually arrested and it was proven that he had broken into seventy homes in nine months. Countless jewels and precious objects were found in his residence. Such a fine person, why become a thief? It's truly incredible.

Correction of "Qiu Shuyuan at the Time of the Cession of Taiwan"

— Liu Shimu

The Northeast is difficult; the barbarian cavalry roams unchecked. The Black River freezes over, causing deep pain in the fields. People with conscience are constantly worried, thinking of ways to strengthen the nation and recover the land. This publication has been collecting stories of our country's past virtuous and heroic figures defending against invaders, to encourage the weak and boost morale. Readers are all deeply moved, wishing they could draw their bows and follow suit. However, the article "Qiu Shuyuan at the Time of the Cession of Taiwan" published on the 27th of last month confuses things, and needs to be corrected. Upon investigation, the "Qiu Shuyuan at the Time of the Cession of Taiwan" article contains all the achievements of Mr. Qiu Fengjia's life. Qiu Fengjia, styled Xian'gen, also known as Canghai and Nanwushanren, was a native of Jiaoling County, Guangdong (formerly Zhenping). His life's deeds are as described in the article: bravely facing national crises, and writing poetry in his later years. His "Lingyun Hairi Lou Poetry Collection" in twelve volumes, was published in the autumn of the second year of the Republic of China, one year after Mr. Fengjia passed away. Mr. Qiu Shuyuan, styled Wei, is a native of Haicheng, Fujian. Although he corresponded with Mr. Fengjia, they never met. Furthermore, he is still alive and resides in Singapore in Southeast Asia. Last year, he served as the editor of the supplement of the Singapore Daily News. Mr. Shuyuan and I are close friends, and we communicate frequently. Mr. Wang Shengzhi, the leader of the Malayan athletes who came to Shanghai last month, is Mr. Shuyuan's worthy son-in-law. Mr. Shuyuan wrote "Five Hundred Stone Cave Heaven Writings" in twelve volumes, published in the twenty-fifth year of Guangxu. His writings and morals are enough to influence the world. However, his poetry and prose do not mention Taiwan. It should be known that he has never set foot on Taiwan. I saw Mr. Fengjia once at my father's residence when I was young. With national crises at hand, reading his works brings back memories. The wise man has passed away, when will we wield our spears again? I cannot help but shed tears. I wonder what Mr. Shuyuan will think when he reads this.

(Note) The deeds of Qiu Fengjia can be found in Qiu Shuyuan's "Five Hundred Stone Cave Heaven Writings," Volume 3, pages 3 to 5.

Record of Names of Martyrs Who Died in the Sino-Japanese War (Part 2)

— Wang Chang

Ding Ruchang, Naval Admiral. In the Battle of the Yalu River that year, almost half of the navy was destroyed. Ruchang gathered the remnants and returned to Weihaiwei. The following year, the enemy attacked Weihai urgently. In the second month, they deployed all their forces at the eastern entrance, repeatedly destroying our ships. The soldiers lacked morale. Ruchang, knowing there was nothing he could do, committed suicide by taking poison.

Liu Buchan, Rear Admiral of the Navy. A native of Houguan. He died from cannon fire (according to the Qing History Museum biography), or by hanging himself, according to another account.

Zhang Wenxuan, General, and Liu Gongang, Military Commander. Both agreed with Ding Ruchang's proposal to perish with the ships. After Ruchang's death, Wenxuan also committed suicide by taking poison. Yang Yonglin, General, styled Yuting. After Weihai fell, Yonglin aimed a pistol at the soft spot in his mouth. The bullet entered his brain, and white pus flowed out of his nostrils, hanging down about a foot. He sat upright and did not fall. The enemy was surprised and thought he was a god. See the biographies of Lin Shu and Xu Jingyan.

Huang Zulian, Commandant, died with Yang Yonglin.

Li Kuiyuan, Commander of the torpedo boat Wang Dengyun. When the Lu Jiaotai fort in Weihai fell, Dengyun fought bravely. Kuiyuan shielded Dengyun with his body and died from a bullet. See Luo Dunrong's "Record of the Destruction of the Weihaiwei Fleet."

Yang Ziyun, Military Assistant in Taiwan to Liu Yongfu. After Taiwan was ceded, the Taiwanese people righteously refused. They planned to defend. The enemy fiercely attacked, but were unsuccessful. Then, treacherous people led them through secret paths, flanking the Taiwanese army. Ziyun fought and slit his throat.

Yuan Xiqing, Commander of the New Chu Army under Li Weiyi. He died in battle at the Dajia River in Tainan.

Wu Pengnian. Pengnian guarded the Dajia River, ambushing and repeatedly defeating the enemy army. Later, after the Dajia River fell, he retreated to Bagua Mountain. The enemy obtained guides from local bandits and attacked. Pengnian fought to the last and died a martyr. Xu Xiang, leader of the righteous people of Tainan. When the enemy attacked the Dajia River, they were defeated by Wu Pengnian and retreated across the river. Xiang set an ambush, attacking them as they were halfway across, annihilating their entire army. Later, he continued to resist, holding out for several months. His army was starving and exhausted. The enemy army then attacked with full force. Xiang fought bravely, always at the front lines. He was eventually killed by cannon fire.

Sun Zitang, son of Sun Kaihua, Admiral of the Fujian Land Forces. His name is missing. Zitang is his courtesy name. He rallied righteous soldiers to resist the enemy. Lacking support, he charged into the enemy lines on horseback, fighting to the death at Sandiao Ridge in Tainan. See the joint biography of the Sun family.

The above are the names of thirty identifiable martyrs. There are countless more whose names are unknown. My knowledge is limited, and I cannot fully commend their loyalty and righteousness. I hope that learned scholars across the country will share their knowledge. I would be most grateful.

Jottings from the Ocean Seas

— Yi Zang

Poor Children Occupy Palace: About forty miles outside the capital of Spain, to the west of the Royal Palace of Alfonso, about two hundred impoverished children recently broke into the palace, occupying the imperial dining hall and bedrooms, gathering to play and laugh. Because the palace was unguarded and the Spanish King was residing in another palace, they were able to invade. It is said that the palace is located about forty miles from Madrid, surrounded by verdant mountains and clear streams, with beautiful scenery. This magnificent palace has now become a slum, which is quite amusing.

Queen Rides Third-Class Train: Queen Helen of Romania and Princess Ileana, the Crown Prince, recently traveled to Scotland on a third-class train in London. At the time, they went unnoticed. Later, it was seen that many British royal nobles were boarding the train to see them off, and it was then revealed to be the Queen of Romania. Everyone was amazed and said, "I wanted to see what third-class trains are like, so I took a ride." News reporters rushed to take pictures, but were all rejected. However, the story has already spread throughout London.

The Louse King

— Rui Yucheng

My friend Mr. Wang Dingwu, previously served in the military in the Northeast for many years. Among his comrades was a "Louse King" who was quite famous for a time, and who eventually died from lice. The other day, Mr. Wang told me the story of the "Louse King," which was quite bizarre. So, I record it here. According to Mr. Wang, lice are transformed from human essence. They easily breed if the body is dirty, because the essence excreted from the sweat glands of the human body, when not washed away for a long time, transforms into lice. Bathrooms are rare in the north, and washing is inconvenient. Therefore, it is very easy for ordinary people to get lice. But they can be removed in a day and night. The method is to hang the clothes in the courtyard. After one night, the lice will all freeze to death. A shake will remove them all. One of Mr. Wang's comrades, named Rong, had a "louse hole" on each side of his waist, the size of a needle's eye. Lice would often crawl out of these holes. Every time Mr. Rong reached to his waist and touched it, dozens of lice would immediately gather in his palm. Because of this, Mr. Wang and others nicknamed him "Louse King." Later, Mr. Rong contracted the disease of "louse prison." This disease name had never been heard before. It is said that this disease is incurable, and those who contract it will die. So, Mr. Rong also died from it. At the moment of death, countless lice emerged from all seven orifices, including the anus and urethra, numbering no less than hundreds of thousands.

A Tale of Two Buildings of Military Affairs (Part 4)

— Master of Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter One: An Unrivaled Courtesan Lives Alone, Cherishing Her Beautiful Companion; A Wanderering Student in a Foreign Land Creates a Strange Romance.

However, this heaven-defying omen was not the kind of superstitious talk that heaven would send down some kind of disaster or calamity upon her. It was just that since heaven had given birth to such a rare beauty, it would naturally endow her with a unique personality of innate intelligence. Although she seemed gentle and docile on the surface, and didn't seem to have much knowledge, she was still a person. And people have thoughts. Thinking and pondering in bits and pieces, referencing and examining, gradually piecing together a whole chain of reasoning, she discovered that she was a person without status, a person who was forced to be called a person just to be a plaything for others. She had no independent personality, no freedom of human rights. Living a life like a caged bird, she also faced the danger of being at the mercy of others' love and hate, and not knowing what would happen when she grew old and her beauty faded. So, she began to fear. She began to be angry. A new thought of urgently wanting to be a person and never being a plaything again was burning like a raging fire in her heart, affecting the strong and passionate personality that she had been suppressing, and it all exploded and manifested. She then displayed her spirit of resistance, exercised her decisive skills, and resolutely sought freedom and fought for liberation, looking like a fighting warrior. Her motives for declaring war and the course of the battle were reported so enthusiastically by major and minor newspapers at the time, like news of the European war, publishing many divergent reports. Although the matter seemed very important, the truth was obscured. No one knew which newspaper had the most accurate information. Fortunately, this is a thing of the past, and there is no need to seek certainty here. To put it simply, for more than half a year, although the old fellow had not been abusive to her, he had too many other favorites, and the old man could not divide himself and often did not accompany her in the small mansion. Occasionally, when he came, he gradually became presumptuous, cold and sarcastic, and did not give her a good look. A few days ago, she went out to a foreign firm and spent a dozen dollars to buy a pair of silk stockings. He found out and嫌她有点浪費。said that she was a little wasteful. He said two sentences to her. Then, he grew tired of her favorite little pug dog and lightly kicked it, causing the dog to bark and bark straight away. She suffered this grievance, clinging to the kicked dog, stroking it frequently, and quietly shedding a few tears. From then on, she never spoke to him again. A few days later, she took the dog and left. She found a lawyer famous for handling divorce cases and sent a formal letter to the old fellow, requesting a divorce. The old fellow saw that the situation was difficult to reverse. Suddenly, he became generous, willing to settle peacefully with her, giving her all the clothes, jewelry, furnishings, and appliances that he had bought for her over the years in the small mansion, and also giving her an additional $30,000 in cash as alimony. Finally, they met one last time.

Financial Gold Price Has Fallen Back

Reactionary Reversal, Down 9.7 Taels: Yesterday, the surge in the gold price subsided, and it softened again. It once returned to within 700 taels, with the situation unclear, seemingly advancing and retreating. There was a difference of more than nine taels between the morning and evening sessions, eventually falling by about ten taels. This was a reaction after several days of continuous rises. Although the opening was down and the large bars continued to fall, the silver price rose instead. Therefore, the sentiment among traders trended downwards. Subsequently, buyers showed courage and the exchange rate turned large, with the British exchange rate shrinking and the American exchange rate loosening. The price immediately rose by more than four taels. Later, rumors spread that American citizens were indignant about the Japanese invasion of North China and opposed Stimson's refusal to handle the matter according to the treaty. Market sentiment weakened further and continued to decline, falling from outside 700 taels to within 696 taels. The market recovered slightly later, but large buyers remained strong, showing signs of profit-taking. Eventually, it rebounded to 700 taels again. Although there was news of reduced production of Indian raw silver and future silver coin replacements, large long positions did not sell off, and there were still many small short positions. Therefore, the price had the potential to hold firm.

The morning market fluctuated, opening down 9.5 taels at 700 taels. Large silver bars fell another 3/8, while the silver price rose 1/8, and private telegrams were slightly 1/8. The Securities Exchange will Reduce Futures Margin Next Week

Also, the Securities Exchange decided to appropriately reduce the futures trading margin starting next week due to the recent trend of stable market prices and slack market conditions. It is set to collect 400 yuan for each 10,000 yuan transaction for both buyers and sellers, 1,000 yuan for special certificates, totaling 1,400 yuan.

Food

River Down Rice: Rising Trend Stabilizes

Few boats arrived in the South Shanghai market yesterday. Urban and rural shops were quiet. Suzhou and Tongbai japonica rice were expensive and stable, while early and late rice saw little demand, with no price increases or decreases. Three loads of foreign Du-style pointed-grain rice were sold entirely on the same day, with prices up five cents, equivalent to two yuan. Dessert shops were the most active, purchasing 600 dan, with prices rising slightly. The weather cleared at Xin Zha Tian Shi, with a source of thirty to forty houses on the west road. The situation was uninspired. Suzhou and Changbei japonica rice prices were initially firm in the morning but turned sluggish in the afternoon, with prices softening by one dime. Thin rice has been falling sharply for days, and future supplies will inevitably be scarce. Du-style pointed grain rice arrivals were not abundant, demand was also quiet, and prices remained unchanged. Glutinous rice trading was brisk, with a stable situation.

The market showed slight weakness, with Xiaoxiao rice for March offered at four liang and four qian, April at four liang and five qian and a half, and May at four liang and seven qian and two and a half fen. Number One Saigon rice for February was offered at five liang, two qian, and six fen.

客秈 rice from Hunan and Jiangxi provinces is no longer available. There is also not much from Anhui province. However, the harvest in Wenzhou and Taizhou is still good. Yesterday, there were new arrivals of Taizhou special white rice, with 588 bags offered at eleven yuan, seven dimes, and four cents. These were also purchased by businesses on this street.

Flour: Initially Strong, Then Weak

Dalian Group Gradually Selling

Flour Exchange Suspends Trading for Ten Days for New Year Holiday

Yesterday, after the market opened in the morning, flour prices for various months showed a slight upward trend due to favorable foreign wheat quotations, rising by about four dimes, and the continuous rise in gold prices, which boosted market confidence. As a result, prices for various months rose by about one fen compared to the previous day. However, trading was not smooth, and actual sales were mostly cautious. After the market opened in the afternoon, trading remained quiet. However, it was reported that the Dalian Group, due to political issues, was facing difficulties in shipping goods and was gradually selling out. Although there was no widespread selling pressure, market sentiment softened again. Given the sluggish actual sales, the outcome for this month is still subject to change. As a result, prices for January and February remained unchanged, March increased by two li and a half, April remained unchanged, May increased by small seven li and a half, and June increased by large two li and a half.

The Flour Exchange will suspend trading for ten days from the 30th of this month until the 10th of February. This has been announced in the market.

Wheat Prices Decline

Exchange Suspends Trading for Thirteen Days from the 28th for New Year Holiday

Yesterday, after the market opened in the morning and afternoon, wheat prices for various months showed a flat and weak trend. As the Lunar New Year approaches, many outside speculators are liquidating their positions. Furthermore, due to the sale of relief wheat, the millers' wheat stocks are becoming more abundant. The supply of raw wheat in the market appears to be dwindling. In this environment, bulls have little room to maneuver. Consequently, prices for this month have been declining step by step. According to observations within the industry, the final outcome may be lower than the prices at the end of last year. Prices for distant months also showed slight weakness. As a result, the price for this month fell by five fen compared to the previous day, February fell by three fen, March and April fell by two fen, May fell by one fen, and June fell by two fen. The Miscellaneous Grains Exchange has decided to suspend trading from the 28th of this month until the 10th of February. It is said that this is due to the need to settle accounts for the Lunar New Year.

Silk and Tea

European and American Silk Markets Increasingly Weak and Quiet

Yesterday, the foreign silk market in this port was weak and quiet. This was due to the extremely low opening prices for raw silk in the European and American markets, resulting in sluggish factory sales. Telegrams from Shanghai were not forwarded, and market sentiment was sluggish. Yesterday, only Chang and other companies purchased 25 bales of white dried silk, with prices remaining flat and weak.

Spring Cocoon Opening Prices Remain High

Each 100 Jin of silk needs to pull out 850-860 liang of silk.

Although sales of white factory silk to Europe and America have been sluggish, cocoon prices have remained firm. This is because the spring cocoon harvest last year was poor in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, and the opening prices for fresh cocoons were not low. The 折頭 (discount) (i.e., the conversion rate from cocoons to silk) was also high, resulting in higher cocoon costs. Cocoon merchants have maintained a firm stance, and cocoon prices remain high. Yesterday, a silk factory in Zhabei purchased 108 dan of Changzhou East Road spring dried cocoons at a price of 171 liang. The conversion rate was 500 jin of silk. Each 100 jin of silk requires 850-860 liang of cocoons.

Wuyuan Zhenmei Tea Already Showing Signs of Activity

Wuyuan North Road Zhenmei tea has always been known for its excellent production methods. Last year, sales to Morocco, Africa, and other markets were sluggish due to the Japanese promoting and undermining its reputation and the competition from cheap Japanese tea. As a result, there were significant stockpiles in the Shanghai market. Recently, Chinese merchants, considering that the Gregorian New Year has passed, have had to repeatedly lower prices in order to sell their goods and recover their funds. Yesterday, Baochang, Tianyu, and other companies purchased over 300 chests, with selling prices around 100 liang, which is 40-50 liang lower than before. Chinese merchants have suffered significant losses.

Hardware: Black Iron Sheet Sales Revive

Trading in black iron sheets was previously brisk due to a shortage of supplies and heavy purchases by various groups. As a result, market prices rose sharply to 11 liang and 5 qian. Later, due to the situation in Tianjin, sales became sluggish. Although various businesses made every effort to promote sales, they were ultimately unable to revive the market due to the unfavorable environment. In recent days, with the colder weather, various groups have resumed purchasing. As a result, transactions have become brisk again. Yesterday, there were a total of 600-700 dan traded, with buyers from the Northern Group and local factories. Although prices have not yet increased significantly, they have improved by two qian compared to before. 18-sheet goods are estimated at 11 liang per dan, and 36-foot goods are offered at 9 liang and 7 qian and a half per dan.

Coal: Kailping Coal Prices Rise Slightly

Since the New Year, Kailping coal prices have been increased by the company due to the limited supply of various types of Kailping coal. The current selling price for Kailping special coal is 11 liang per ton, which is 5 qian higher than before. Kailping Number One coal is 10 liang per ton, and Number Two coal is 9 liang, 2 qian and 5 fen, each rising 2 qian and a half. Kailping lump coal has also risen 5 qian, currently selling for 11 liang per ton. Market traders are offering prices with an additional 2 qian and a half to 5 qian per ton.

Local News

Wang Zhaoming's Telegram Replies to Chen Mingshu

Details Reasons for Resigning from Standing Committee

Wang Jingwei, who is ill in the hospital, telegraphed Chen Mingshu of Nanjing yesterday, saying: "To Vice President Chen Xun of the Nanjing Executive Yuan: I have received your telegram and am deeply grateful. Since my departure, I have been ill in bed and have repeatedly received your concerns. You are very familiar with my condition and treatment methods, so it goes without saying that I am not using illness as an excuse to shirk responsibility. However, given my current condition, I am unable to travel. In recent days, many comrades from various parties have come to see me. Refusing to see them often leads to misunderstandings, while meeting them results in serious issues being raised that often exceed the doctor's prescribed time. For this reason, I have repeatedly experienced dizziness. From this, it can be inferred that even if my own life is not worth cherishing, using a confused mind to deal with complex events would harm the party and the country, which is a great concern. This is similar to a wounded soldier who needs time to heal. Driving them to the battlefield would only lead to their defeat. Since I have been re-elected as a Central Executive Committee member by the congress, I dare not lightly abandon my responsibility. However, the Standing Committee, by its very name, requires daily attendance to handle daily affairs. Now that I am unable to do so due to illness, I should submit a request to the Central Party Headquarters and the Political Council to be relieved of this position. The telegram has already been sent, and I hope you will understand. Although I am bedridden and my situation is different from yours, our well-being is closely linked. If I can recover quickly, I will have more time to make up for my shortcomings. Please also convey this to my brothers, Zhesheng and others. Wang Zhaoming, Geng."

Feng Yuxiang Visited Wang Yesterday to Urge Him to Stay

Following Wang Jingwei's telegram to Nanjing resigning from his positions on the Central Party Headquarters and the Standing Committee of the Political Council, National Government Member Feng Yuxiang personally visited Wang at Nar Hospital on Avenue Joffre at 4:15 PM yesterday to express his sympathy and earnestly urge him to stay. The two men spoke for about half an hour before Feng left at 4:50 PM. It is reported that Wang's condition has not improved and he still experiences dizziness, so he intends to firmly resign. As for Feng's trip to Hong Kong, he telegraphed Hu Zhantang a few days ago to inquire about his views and arrange a date. He will leave Shanghai for the south as soon as he receives Hu's reply.

Feng Yuxiang's Admonitory Letter to Subordinates

Feng Yuxiang recently sent a letter to one of his subordinates, admonishing them on various matters. The tone is very sincere. The letter is excerpted below: (Omitted part) "I thank you for sending someone from afar to see me. All letters and details of the military situation have been forwarded by Comrade so-and-so, and I am very pleased to know them well. To reciprocate your kindness, I would like to share some of my insights with you, which may be helpful to you in these difficult times for the country. I will list several points below: (1) Defending the country is the duty of us soldiers, and we should always be mindful of national humiliation and national crisis, and always be prepared to avenge and relieve the crisis. We must not avoid danger and fear hardship, and eliminate the ambition of soldiers and abandon the duty of soldiers. We should think that this is the time for soldiers to serve the country. In the past hundred years, the humiliation our country has suffered has been extreme. More than 3 million square miles of land have been lost, and 30 million compatriots have been enslaved. The loss of property is not counted, and our compatriots who have been captured are being raped and killed by the Japanese army every day. Who has no parents, who has no siblings, who is not heartbroken by the devastation? As recently reported, the Japanese army entered Jin and searched and killed more than 3,000 soldiers and students at one time, not to mention other incidents. This is the actual damage our country has suffered. The Japanese propaganda abroad is even more disrespectful to us. Fangze and Inuyakii, etc., said that China is only a country in name, and does not actually qualify as a country. Biyuan said that there will never be war between China and Japan, because Chinese soldiers are all softbones and do not know what a country is. My brother, can you not be heartbroken when you hear this? I hope that my brother will continue to uphold our usual patriotic enthusiasm, encourage the soldiers, and swear to avenge this shame, so as not to be ashamed of being a soldier, and so as not to be unworthy of the people's support. My brother, strive to serve the country today. If you do not work hard now, I am afraid that you will want to save your country and love it after the country is destroyed. (2) To serve the country and the people, we must never forget the country and the people, and we must put all our own interests out of the question. Only by benefiting the country and the people, and not seeking benefits for ourselves, can we be called revolutionaries, and can we discuss the doctrine of revolution. In this way, we will not fail the country and the people in the public sphere, and we will also complete our own immortal career in the private sphere. The whole point is the distinction between public and private, which must first be clarified. (3) True and false are certain, and there is no room for doubt. For example, training troops is for protecting the country and defending the people, for the public and not for the private. Discipline must be strict, physical strength must be healthy, and soldiers must share weal and woe. All hobbies must be cut off. Also, whatever officers want soldiers to abide by, officers must first abide by, and if they want soldiers to be unafraid of death, generals must be unafraid of death. These are all truths, all true and false. Conversely, if generals do what soldiers are not allowed to do, then there is no right and wrong. If right and wrong are not clear, even if a person deals with things in the world, he will not be respected or trusted, and he will definitely fail. How can we not be cautious about such a major matter as governing an army? (4) 'The people are the foundation of the country' has been said for thousands of years. In democratic countries today, the people are the masters, and we should pay more attention to the people. Everything must be aimed at the interests of the people, and there must be no oppression of the people, and there must be no disrespect for the people. We must know that the parents of officers and soldiers are the people, and the brothers of officers and soldiers are the people, that is, the relatives, friends, neighbors, and countrymen of officers and soldiers, all of whom are the people. Loving and respecting the people is loving and respecting our own parents, brothers, relatives, friends, neighbors, and countrymen. In particular, we must know that the suffering of the people has mostly become an inhuman life, so how can we bear to oppress them again? Not to mention that the oppressed people will inevitably resist, even with our conscience, we should not oppress them. In addition, there are other friends, that is, in order to unite all parties and unite against foreign enemies, we only ask for sincerity and joint efforts to save the country. We have no other desires. I am in the position of an ordinary citizen, doing my duty, and have no hope of wielding military power again. I only hope that you will sincerely work hard, diligently do your duty, revitalize yourself, promote yourself, and spur yourself on to become a simple and hardworking patriotic soldier. I am willing and satisfied. Of course, I will do my best to help you with other things. Don't worry about it."

Will Advise Hu Jining in a Personal Capacity

Tan Zhen's Important Remarks

Wang, Hu, Jiang, and Sun All Share Responsibility for Practical Politics

The Government Takes Public Opinion as Its Guide and Does Not Use the Military as a Background

The Far Eastern News Agency reports that Tan Liming, the Vice President of the Legislative Yuan, who recently arrived in Shanghai and is staying at the Cangzhou Hotel, made important remarks to a reporter from the Far Eastern News Agency who visited him regarding the establishment of the new government. He said that the new government was officially established on New Year's Day, but because Mr. Wang, Mr. Hu, and Mr. Jiang have not yet come to Nanjing to participate, many people speculate that the new government's foundation may not be solid because the three gentlemen have not taken responsibility in Nanjing. In fact, the establishment of the new government is based on the party's sincere unity and the people's desire for peace and unity. Although the new government's center of gravity seems to be the responsibility of the President of the Executive Yuan, Mr. Sun Zhesheng, the Executive Yuan only assumes administrative responsibility, and the Executive Yuan's policy must be subject to the Central Executive Committee, and the Central Executive Committee's guidance of the political machine is the Central Political Council. Mr. Wang, Mr. Hu, and Mr. Jiang are all standing committee members of the Central Political Council, so Mr. Wang, Mr. Hu, and Mr. Jiang all share the responsibility for the highest political guidance. Moreover, Mr. Sun Zhesheng's resolute entry into Nanjing, taking on arduous tasks, and shouldering administrative responsibilities is the common will and joint recommendation of Mr. Wang, Mr. Hu, and Mr. Jiang. However, the power and will are often unable to be concentrated and unified. This is an undeniable fact. This time, the comrades inside and outside the party, because of the increasing foreign aggression and the imminent national disaster, must sincerely unite in order to seek unity, and without unity, they cannot resist foreign aggression. Therefore, comrades from all parties, under the strict supervision of the people of the whole country, have abandoned their prejudices, cooperated, and jointly elected Mr. Sun Zhesheng as the President of the Executive Yuan. This move is completely based on factual needs, because sincere unity means that the comrades of our party share the responsibility of building the country. Mr. Wang, Mr. Hu, and Mr. Jiang have always been in a guiding position in politics, and they must now express that they share responsibility, so it is not appropriate for any one of the three to take on the actual political responsibility alone. Therefore, we sincerely hope that they will all come to Nanjing as soon as possible to decide on the party and government policies of the central government. However, whether they come to Nanjing or not, they will still have political responsibility, because they cannot shirk their responsibility in the past history, and now the Central Political Council is composed of the three gentlemen as standing committee members, and Mr. Sun Zhesheng as the President of the Executive Yuan, which is also jointly elected by the three gentlemen. In recent days, not long after the establishment of the new government, there have been many speculations and rumors. In fact, the new government was established at a time when the people's minds were wavering. This situation may be unavoidable. However, Chinese politics is greatly affected by the wavering of the people's minds. Some people often cannot calmly observe the political situation and make rational judgments, and they are easily shaken. Cunning people take advantage of this kind of unstable psychology to fuel the flames and hinder the government's policies. Taking the establishment of the new government as an example, since the new government is generated by the party's sincere unity and the people's expectations, the people should trust and support it. They cannot make random speculations just because Mr. Wang, Mr. Hu, and Mr. Jiang have not yet arrived in Nanjing. Under the complex environment inside and outside, only this newly established government can stabilize the interior, and only by stabilizing the interior can we resist foreign aggression. Also, such as the recent rumors about the nine-province joint defense, Minister He Yingqin has denied that there is no such thing. However, people have been spreading rumors, and there is a general idea that division and internal strife are about to come. This situation can prove the people's desire to end the chaos, but I hope that the people will observe calmly and not be too nervous. The new government believes that at a time when foreign troubles are increasing, no one will dare to defy the people of the whole country, otherwise they will be despised by the people. As for the Chinese military, they have always held their guns to coerce everything and threaten the government. This phenomenon is entirely due to the fact that those in power in the past wanted to use force to unify the country. The members of the new government dare to express their firm will, that is, to absolutely not rely on the strength of any one military to support politics. We have no military as a background, and we will never want to use the military. The foundation of the new government is built on the great transition of all party comrades and the trust and support of the people of the whole country. In the future, we will adhere to this principle, take public opinion as our guide, and seek self-reliance. Also, such as the establishment of political sub-committees in the two provinces of Guangdong and Guangxi, although there have been records in the newspapers in recent days, many people have proposed this matter at the Fourth Plenary Session, and they have not had time to study it in detail. The resolution was handed over to the Standing Committee for verification and handling, and there will be a solution in the future. Furthermore, the statement published by the soldiers in the Northeast was not signed and cannot be immediately recognized as a fact. In short, the new government was established in an unstable environment for the people, and various doubts are inevitable. However, I hope that the people will observe the politics more calmly in the future, and urge and support the government with enthusiasm, so as to jointly complete this current task. As for Mr. Wang, Mr. Hu, and Mr. Jiang, we hope that they can all come to Nanjing as soon as possible and share the difficult tasks with their colleagues. However, whether they come to Nanjing or not, they will still be responsible for the actual government. As for the armed comrades, I hope that they will work hard to prepare for national defense, pay attention to local pacification, do their duty, and not make claims against the government at will, make criticisms at will, and should absolutely obey the government's orders. This government has been jointly promoted by all party comrades and the people of the whole country.

Taiwanese Émigrés Longing for the Motherland

The Suffering of Taiwanese Compatriots... The Motherland Faces Imminent Danger

Compatriots, Rise Up Quickly... Willing to Provide Support

A Respectful Announcement from the Taiwanese Émigré Association to All Compatriots Throughout the Country: We humbly believe that since Taiwan was ceded to Japan by our motherland after the defeat in the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-95, forty years have passed. At that time, our three million compatriots, in order to satiate the greed of the fierce enemy and save the motherland from collapse and peril, swallowed their voices and shed tears, becoming slaves to others. We originally hoped that the motherland would learn from this experience, strive for self-improvement, and seek to govern well so as to wipe away the humiliation and seek revenge, so that Taiwanese compatriots could one day see the light of day again. Unexpectedly, in the past twenty-odd years, the government has become more and more corrupt, the country more and more chaotic, the military more and more numerous, and the country more and more weakened. Recently, Liaoning and Jilin were lost in less than three days, allowing the ancestral enemy, the Japanese bandits, to trample upon the four northeastern provinces. The whole country is horrified and wishes to fight to the death. However, the authorities of the motherland are only preoccupied with dealing with internal party and political disputes, and externally only want to rely on the League of Nations, the organ of the great powers for dividing spoils, to seek compromise and gain. Therefore, after two months of delay, they only managed to send personnel to investigate. Japanese troops invaded Longjiang to the north, but could not be stopped, and disturbed Jinzhou and Yulin to the west, but could not be resisted. It seems that they will allow twenty million compatriots to once again be subjected to the island nation's slavery. When our compatriots heard the news, they were filled with grief. If the three eastern provinces can be abandoned, then what is to prevent the three western provinces, the three northern provinces, and the three southern provinces from being regarded as border provinces and abandoned accordingly? If Japan can take three provinces, what is to prevent Britain, Russia, America, and France from each taking the three provinces they desire? If the motherland, though large, can be completely lost in less than five years, what hope is there for us Taiwanese compatriots? Today, our four hundred million compatriots no longer have the opportunity to endure hardship and bide our time for revenge. We can hope to fight, but we will surely perish if we do not fight. In the past, when Taiwan was ceded, Tang, Qiu, Liu, and other gentlemen still established a republic and fought for a year, killing tens of thousands of Japanese. In the subsequent thirty-odd years, we Taiwanese, empty-handed, launched twenty-five revolutions. This shows that our people are not incapable of fighting. This time, the authorities of the motherland, fearing the Japanese's strength and violence, advocated non-resistance and calmness, and retreated thousands of miles. However, General Ma Zhanshan's lone army fought bravely and repeatedly thwarted the enemy's advance, standing firm outside the borders to this day, unyielding. This shows that our army is not incapable of fighting. As for internal political and party disputes, these are just family matters between brothers. If each side yields a little, what is there that cannot be resolved? Otherwise, please come to Taiwan and see the suffering of four million compatriots who are being trampled upon by foreigners and made slaves to foreigners. Then, what resentment and hatred could not be dispelled? Alas, the situation is urgent, the country is in danger! Peace or war should be decided by public opinion, and all policies should be decided by the whole people. This simple and direct approach is truly the most important plan for today. We hope that our four hundred million compatriots will rise up quickly and plan for it. Our four million Taiwanese compatriots, due to the various policies of isolation imposed by the Japanese, have been almost forgotten by the people of the motherland for the past twenty-odd years. Furthermore, because one or two unfilial sons have been exploited by the Japanese in Xiamen and Fujian, committing evil deeds in the name of the enemy, the people of the motherland have fallen for the Japanese's divisive tactics and often harbor contempt for the entire group, not regarding them as ordinary overseas Chinese. They do not know that our four million compatriots sacrificed their human rights in the past to save the motherland. Today, not only is their conduct not free, but there are no Chinese schools on the island. New Chinese ideas and party doctrines are completely banned, and they are not allowed to enter. However, the authorities of the motherland do not observe this. In successive national representative conferences, our island's four million overseas Chinese do not have a single fixed quota, treating them as uncivilized and stubborn people, just like the former Qing dynasty. The Japanese bandits are secretly pleased by this. However, the feelings of our Taiwanese compatriots for the motherland have never diminished. Those with education and aspirations have returned to the country to serve year after year, spreading throughout the political, academic, military, commercial, medical, industrial, and agricultural circles of the central and southern provinces. There are countless people who have made special and continuous contributions. However, in order to protect their relatives and avoid the Japanese's surveillance, they have all changed their names and adopted ancestral origins, so people do not notice. This time, with the outbreak of the national crisis in the Northeast, Taiwanese compatriots throughout the island are even more deeply saddened and indignant. They send people back to their hometowns, avoiding the enemy's eyes and ears, to inquire about how to act in concert with the compatriots of the motherland. Compatriots, strive! We hope that all, from top to bottom, will be of one mind, abandon private views, and quickly decide on a war resolution, establishing a military force to recover the lost territories and rescue twenty million compatriots from fire and water. Although we Taiwanese compatriots are not clever, we will surely have ways to provide support for the motherland. As I write, I am filled with grief and do not know what to say. Respectfully announced by the Taiwanese Émigré Association in December of the 20th year of the Republic of China.

Opinions on National Salvation from All Sectors

A Telegram from the National Salvation Association to the National Government of the Republic of China: We respectfully submit to the Nanjing National Government: After the fall of Jinzhou, this association has four proposals: (1) Ma Zhanshan was able to resist Japan with a lone army, while Zhang Xueliang was unable to resist Japan with a large army. We request that clear orders be issued to reward and punish them separately. This is the first point. (2) Zhang Fakui telegraphed to support Heilongjiang, Feng Yuxiang strongly advocated fighting Japan, Yan Xishan advocated mobilizing troops, and He Yingqin telegraphed requesting mobilization. We request that clear orders be issued to implement these measures. This is the second point. (3) Currently, Shanhaiguan is in imminent danger. While urgently addressing the symptoms, it is also necessary to address the root cause. Since Feng Yuxiang is the most vigorous advocate of war and Zhang Xueliang has difficulty resisting the enemy, we request that the troops be transferred to Feng's command, and that all departments in the Northwest and Northeast be uniformly designated as National Salvation Armies, vowing to declare war and recover the territory within a fixed time, so as to avert the crisis. At the same time, dispatch elite troops as reinforcements. This is the third point. (4) Many plans were made before the establishment of the new government, but after its establishment, there were still no concrete measures, greatly disappointing the people. Since the tragic loss of the Northeast, the people of the country have said that the former government misled the country. Now that Jinzhou has not been defended, the new government can hardly escape its blame. From now on, we request that it bear full responsibility for diplomatic measures, the recovery of territory, and the resettlement of the people. This is the fourth point. During the National Congress, this association formally submitted a petition, and during the First Plenary Session of the Central Committee, it proposed six national salvation plans, which Central Committee member Wu Tiecheng fully accepted in principle. Now that the national crisis is becoming more and more dangerous, the millions of troops in the country have more than enough strength to resist Japan and suppress the communists. If there is further delay and indecision, we will inevitably perish together. However, the country belongs to four hundred million people, and it is imperative that we rise up to save ourselves. In addition to establishing branch associations in various places to unite the people and preparing a National Salvation Army based on the first telegram, this association requests clear instructions on whether the four proposals are appropriate. We urge you to respond without delay, as Shanhaiguan may not be able to be defended, and the country may be destroyed in less than ten minutes. Survival is at stake at this moment. We hope that all compatriots and comrades in the country will rise up quickly, pursue the enemy directly, unite to save the country, and not delay. Respectfully, the National Salvation Association of the Republic of China, Qi Yin.

Zhang Xueliang presented Jinzhou as a New Year's gift, handing it over with both hands. He Chengjun revived the old trick of nine-province joint defense with new variations, harboring ulterior motives. The great disaster in the Northeast continues, while the storms in the Southwest intensify. Internal strife ignores external threats, and external threats do not forget internal strife. Alas, what kind of nation has the Chinese nation become? What kind of rulers are those in power? Today, the power of life and death of the Chinese nation rests entirely in your hands. If you do not destroy China, no one can destroy China. We ask you to save China, for no one else can save China. Our four hundred million compatriots entrust their lives to you all. Now, the strong enemy is invading deeper and deeper, but your conflicts have not lessened because of this. The national crisis is becoming more and more urgent, but your actions are becoming slower and slower. We ask, who is responsible for the increasing phenomenon of disintegration today? Although the violent Japanese are fierce, their skills are limited to attacking cities and seizing land; they cannot divide our brothers or separate our compatriots. Alas, will world history not write in large letters two hundred years from now, "It was the Chinese who destroyed China"? When the Premier was on his deathbed, he earnestly instructed us, "Peaceful struggle to save China." Did he mean to use peace to deal with external enemies and internal strife to save China? Today, there is no peace to be had with external enemies, and we retreat step by step. There is a need for peace internally, but swords are drawn and bows are strung. Internal strife should be resolutely avoided, but we insist on fighting. We should fight external enemies urgently, but we lower our banners and silence our drums. Everything is so frustrating that we want to cry but cannot, and want to laugh but cannot. You all, the time is urgent, the situation is pressing! Lay down the butcher's knife of internal strife, and you can become Buddhas on the spot. Cooperate in spirit to thank the people of the country. Rise up quickly to eliminate the strong enemy. This is the only way for you and the four hundred million people to survive together. Old accounts must not be settled again, and new realizations must be made. We have said all we can, and we will wait with tears in our eyes. The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of Shanghai University, Yu.

A Telegram from the 26th Branch of the Municipal Federation: The 26th Branch of the Municipal Federation telegraphed to Chairman Lin of the National Government, Premier Sun of the Executive Yuan, and Central Committee members Wang, Hu, Jiang, and others, stating: Since the September 18th Incident, the people of the whole country have been appealing to all parties, requesting unity to jointly face the national crisis. After exhausting our strength and shouting until we lost our voices for three or four months, we finally achieved a unified government. The people looked forward to it like the re-emergence of the sun and the moon, celebrating with tears in our eyes, thinking that from now on we could unite to save the country. However, from the time of the incident until now, a long time has passed, and the three provinces have been allowed to be lost. The people are in dire straits, living under the iron heel, enduring pain and shedding tears. The troops in the country are stationed and ignore the people's pleas. The people demand that troops be sent to resist, but their requests are ignored. They are left with empty hands and empty calls, waiting patiently for the unified government to implement a plan to save the country. Now, it is reported that some members of the National Government have not yet taken office, or have taken office but are scattered and irresponsible. Central Committee members Wang, Hu, and Jiang are especially watched by China and foreign countries, and are critical to the stability of the country. At this time of national crisis, they should quickly go to the capital to jointly lead the central government, so that those who are generally hesitant to move forward can also be revitalized and jointly plan the country's affairs. Is it that after three of our country's twenty-two provinces have been lost, we do not want to protect the other provinces? And now does the government want to continue to sit and watch? We do not understand to what degree the Central Committee members must see the country destroyed before they can have a change of heart and save the country's people, preferring to be heroes of a destroyed country rather than slaves of a conquered nation. All who have blood and qi share this sentiment. The country's destruction is imminent. We quickly hope that the Central Committee members will share the difficulties with the country, be of one heart and one mind, and quickly decide on a plan to save the country. Time will not come again, so do not delay. We respectfully look forward to your reply. The 16th Branch of the Municipal Federation, Kou Geng.

Wu Zhihao's Opinions on National Salvation

Wu Zhihao sent a letter to the National Federation of Commerce and the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, stating: I respectfully submit that since the founding of the Republic of China, twenty-one years have passed with frequent disasters and repeated famines. There has been no peaceful year. As a result, the people are unable to make a living and the country's strength is declining day by day. Looking back, I cannot help but tremble with fear. Now, the fires of war in the Northeast are raging day and night, and our beautiful rivers and mountains have fallen into the hands of foreign lands. If we do not sleep with our weapons as pillows and wait for dawn to strike down the strong enemy, then the vast land of China will be destroyed and the Chinese people will all be reduced to barbarians. I, Zhihao, am just a merchant and do not know the art of governance, but I dare not lag behind others in my patriotic zeal. I humbly submit my limited views based on the principle that every citizen is responsible for the rise and fall of the world, and earnestly request that your association invite sages from all walks of life to discuss them together: (1) Governance: The strength or weakness of a country depends on its internal affairs, and the goodness or badness of its internal affairs depends on its governance. What has been the governance of our country in the past twenty years has already been shown to the people. Now, for the sake of consolidating the country and ensuring social stability, it is imperative to learn from the past, change course, work hard to govern well, and put things on the right track. As for the steps to be taken, those in power must first abandon past grievances, set a common goal, divide labor and cooperate, and pacify the country to resist foreign enemies. With this spirit of great fearlessness, we can achieve the goal of the world belonging to all. Civil and military officials should encourage each other not to love money and not to fear death, so that the evils of corruption can be eliminated and the responsibility of defending the territory can be fulfilled. However, the affairs of state are complex and there may be shortcomings in the measures taken. Therefore, it is appropriate to gather talents from various provinces to organize political discussion bodies, so that each can express their views and do their best. We can gather small things and think widely to increase the benefits, and even pick up what has been left out and fill in the gaps. Even social conditions and public sentiment can be communicated upwards without being blocked. Only then can governance be cleared up, internal affairs be rectified, and the foundation of prosperity and strength be laid. (2) National Defense: At this time when might makes right, we should pay attention to national defense. Our country has been taught by the gunboat policy of the great powers for decades, but as time passes, we forget. Even with the September 18th Incident, three months have passed and several provinces have been lost. The enemy is raging like fire, and there is a tendency to penetrate deep into our territory, while our policies are divided and we have not fired a single arrow. We are no different from the people of Qin and Yue who look at each other's fat and lean. The country raises more than two million soldiers, and the annual expenditure is not small. Now that the country is in such a crisis, we are sitting by and watching the success or failure, each defending our own territory. Alas, how sad! Therefore, for the sake of the country's survival, it is imperative to rectify national defense, break the feudal ideology, actively train the soldiers of the whole country, replenish military equipment, and prepare early. There must also be a unified command so that we can unanimously resist foreign enemies without the worry of disrupting our own steps. We should also warn each other not to engage in internal strife, lest we invite foreign insults. All the martyrs who have sacrificed for the country over the years should be commended and their families should be comforted, so as to honor the meritorious and encourage the active soldiers to devote themselves to defending the country and guarding the territory. (3) Autonomy: The modern trend of autonomy is becoming more and more turbulent. Although the Three People's Principles of the Premier and the Outline of National Construction are of all kinds, they all point to democracy. Now that our party is adhering to these teachings and governing the country with the party, the policy of administration should be to implement autonomy, so that our party and country are built on the people, so as to achieve the goal of the people owning, governing, and enjoying the country. As for the village and neighborhood system, it is the fundamental basis of autonomy and should be promoted as much as possible to establish the foundation. For local construction matters, such as education, water conservancy, agriculture, industry, and hygiene, those that should be promoted and those that should be reformed should be carried out gradually. In addition, commercial groups and defense corps are necessary for self-defense and should also be organized by the local people. Once we go to war with foreign enemies, we can also prepare to defend against the enemy. Also, in recent years, disasters have been reported repeatedly, and all industries have been in decline. The number of unemployed vagrants is increasing day by day, and if they are not appeased, there will be endless troubles. Therefore, it is imperative to set up factories for vagrants and beggars to accommodate them, so that consumers can devote themselves to production. This is also an important task of autonomy. (4) Laws and Regulations: Our country has a vast territory, surpassing the globe. Customs and folk customs vary, making it difficult for legislators. It is difficult to apply the same laws and regulations to the whole country. Therefore, when legislating, we must consult widely and consider carefully, striving to suit the people's feelings and promote their interests, so that the people can enjoy the protection of the law. Otherwise, we will be making things behind closed doors, only making the people subject to the restrictions of the law and suffering from it. The unscrupulous will also manipulate the law and seek personal gain. Therefore, we must be careful when legislating, and there should be certainty. Do not change things frequently. It is better to be simple and easy to implement than to be dense and incomplete. (5) Finance: Our country's finances are tight, more so than ever. We must make great efforts to rectify them in order to cultivate the foundation of the country. For example, reorganizing domestic and foreign public debts and redrafting tax rules are the most fundamental tasks. As far as taxation is concerned, it is appropriate to increase consumption taxes and luxury taxes to enrich the national treasury (for example, the national consumption of cigarettes reaches more than 200 million yuan per year, and the current unified tax rate is 50% of the value. If we levy an additional 30%, that is, 80% of the value, we can increase tax revenue by 60 million yuan per year, which can be deposited and used for national salvation and disaster relief. Although it is said to be a heavy punishment, it will not harm the people), implement protection taxes and dumping taxes to maintain the development of industry and resist the import of foreign goods. All redundant agencies and tax collection agencies that are different in name but the same in reality should be cut to save public funds and severely punish corruption to deter others. As for the receipt and expenditure of finance, it must be absolutely open and subject to public supervision. Administrative expenses must be handled in strict compliance with the budget and must not be treated as a mere formality, so that floating expenses can be saved and there is no concealment of funds. The way to financial wealth can be expected. (6) Diplomacy: There is no justice in the world, and the country is in the midst of disaster. We should carefully select diplomatic talents and expand international diplomatic funding. We should also actively carry out international propaganda and unite with countries that treat us equally to fight together. (7) Education: Our people's intelligence is shallow due to the lack of universal education, so we should pay attention to popular education to improve the level of the people. For those who are poor, we should set up compulsory schools to accommodate them, and set up mobile schools and cram schools so that those who have lost their studies have the opportunity to be educated. We should promote old morals to build the people's psychology. As for the primary school curriculum, it must be agriculturalized and industrialized to develop the habit of hard work and endurance. Above the middle school level, it should be scientific to make learning practical and encourage military education to establish the foundation of conscription. Those who have excellent grades should be rewarded and allowed to enter middle schools and universities free of charge to encourage them and create talents. (8) Industry: Our country's industry is young and the economy is backward. If we want to become rich and strong, we must revitalize industry. The mining, shipping, fishing, and electrical industries that have already been established should be maintained by the government and should not be destroyed or nationalized. Those that have been nationalized but have been suspended or poorly managed in the middle should be returned to private ownership so that people's industries have full protection and are happy to operate. We should also encourage the financial community to invest in agricultural, industrial, and commercial industries to support their development. If the people cannot afford to do it, the government should do its best to help them succeed. If this is done for several years, the future of industry will surely be prosperous, and the people's livelihood problems can also be solved. (9) People's Food: Our country is an agricultural country, and farmers account for about 300 million people. In recent years, due to the impact of the war, there has been a shortage of food for the people, and the social economy has been exhausted. Since the floods in various provinces last year, the people's livelihood has become more difficult, and Lai Su is eager to come, so we must quickly prepare for the aftermath. We should build dikes, dredge rivers, and promote water conservancy, promote forests to regulate the climate, and guide Huai and guide the river should be carried out actively. We should also reorganize the social warehouses to prepare for famine and set up farmers' loans to benefit. If the year is good, the people will be prosperous and the country will be prosperous. (10) Thrift: Extravagance is a great scourge of society, especially since our country's industry is young, so we must be wary of extravagance. Therefore, those in power should take the lead in promoting thrift, so that those above will imitate those below and develop a simple style. The livelihood of the people of the whole country has reached the point of exhaustion. If those in power do not promote thrift, I am afraid that the national economy will be on the verge of bankruptcy. As far as politicians are concerned, it is difficult to expect them to be honest and incorruptible in this extravagant environment. The above are the few things I can see, and I respectfully ask for your public decision on whether they are appropriate.

Local News Two

Robbery of More Than a Thousand Dollars in a Hail of Bullets

Robbers Had Prearranged

Stole a Box of Wages

The Japanese-owned Xihe Cotton Mill on Robert Road in western Shanghai was preparing to distribute wages at about 3:10 AM yesterday (the 8th) when a large number of robbers suddenly appeared in a hail of bullets and robbed 1,744 yuan in cash. The details of the incident are recorded below:

Mill Situation: The Japanese-owned Xihe Cotton Mill on Robert Road, near the Suzhou Creek in western Shanghai, formerly known as Baocheng Cotton Mill, has been taken over by Japanese businessmen and is divided into factories 1, 2, 3, and 4. The factory covers a wide area and the internal equipment is quite magnificent. There are more than 4,000 male and female workers in the four factories. Business has been very developed in recent years. Although it has suffered considerable losses due to the impact of boycotts, it has endured the pain and continued to operate as usual.

Wage Distribution: The mill is large in scale and has many workers. As a rule, wages are distributed on the first and fifteenth days of the lunar calendar. Day workers are distributed during the day, and night workers are distributed at midnight. Yesterday happened to be the date of wage distribution. At about 3:00 AM (that is, in the second half of the night), the accountant of the mill first finished distributing wages to the night workers in Factory 1 and led the porters to carry four wooden boxes containing more than 10,000 yuan in cash, intending to distribute them in Factories 2, 3, and 4 in turn.

Hail of Bullets: Factories 1 and 2 are only separated by a road. As the porters carried the wooden boxes on their shoulders and had just left the factory gate, suddenly in the dark, gunshots rang out in the distance, and bullets rained down, hitting one after another. The porters were all frightened. They saw a large number of robbers holding mortar guns swarming in. The volunteer police of the mill and the police of the Sixth District nearby heard the sound and rushed to open fire with pistols and bombard the crowd. For a time, there was a hail of bullets on both sides, with as many as sixty or seventy shots. However, the robbers had superior firepower and actually robbed two wooden boxes and dared to resist arrest. The police also tried their best to disregard their own safety and fired as they pursued. Seeing the situation was urgent, the robbers abandoned one box on the ground and robbed one box (the box contained at least 1,744 yuan). They fled in the dark, and fortunately no one was injured.

Unsuccessful Pursuit: The chief of the Sixth District, Ren Lixing, heard the alarm and immediately led Inspector Xu and a large number of police officers to the scene. It happened that Officer Gu of the first police station in charge was leading the police to pursue the robbers. They immediately joined forces to encircle and pursue the robbers. However, at that time, the weather was cold and the night was dark, and the area was remote. The robbers had fled far away without a trace. Until dawn, more than twenty bullet casings were found on the ground outside the factory. After Ren District Chief conducted a detailed inspection, the factory opened a list to report to the署. Ren District Chief immediately ordered the resident detective team and the affiliated police station chiefs and police to apprehend the stolen goods and robbers within a limited time, without delay.

City Detective Team Arrested Eleven Kidnappers

Disguised as Travelers with Families Opening Rooms

Surveilled Movements and Arrested Zhang Xinfu

The captain of the city's detective team, Lu Ying, received a secret report the other day, saying that a large number of kidnappers were hiding in the Changxing Hotel at 281-283 Caishi Street and the Nanyang Hotel at 94 Xixinqiao Street next door in the French Concession. One of the bandits, named Zhang Xinfu (nickname "Little Cobbler," from Zhenjiang), was the mastermind behind the kidnapping of Zhang Xiaoliang, the owner of the Jiu Ji Timber Firm on Jichang Street in the Nanshi District, last year. Please send personnel to arrest them as soon as possible. After hearing the report, Captain Lu secretly dispatched a detective the night before, accompanied by his female family members, disguised as a traveler to the Changxing Hotel, opened room 22, and surveyed the movements of these people. Until about 11:00 PM last night, Captain Lu personally led the entire team of detectives, together with the detectives from the French Concession Police, to encircle and arrest them. Eight people were arrested in room 54 of the Changxing Hotel, and three people were intercepted in Nanyang. "Little Cobbler" Zhang Xinfu was indeed among them. They were immediately taken to the police station. After a brief interrogation by the police chief, Captain Lu took them to the Public Security Bureau and detained them for detailed interrogation.
